 sūtraprasthānam  anuvyākhyānam nārāyaṇaṃ nikhilapūrṇaguṇaikadehaṃ nirdoṣamāpyatamamapyakhilaiḥ suvākyaiḥ asyodbhavādidamaśeṣaviśeṣato pi vandyaṃ sadā priyatamaṃ mama sannamāmi  MAnuv tameva śāstraprabhavaṃ praṇamya jagadgurūṇāṃ gurumañjasaiva viśeṣato me paramākhyavidyāvyākhyāṃ karomyanvapi cāhameva  MAnuv prādurbhūto harirvyāso viriñcabhavapūrvakaiḥ arthitaḥ paravidyākhyaṃ cakre śāstramanuttamam  MAnuv gururgurūṇāṃ prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇāṃ bādarāyaṇaḥ yatastaduditaṃ mānamajādibhyastadarthataḥ  MAnuv vaktṛśrotṛprasaktīnāṃ yadāptiranukūlatā āptavākyatayā tena śrutimūlatayā tathā  MAnuv yuktimūlatayā caiva prāmāṇyaṃ trividhaṃ mahat dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇāmekadhānyatra sarvaśaḥ  MAnuv ato naitādṛśaṃ kiñcit pramāṇatamamiṣyate svayaṃ kṛtāpi tadvayākhyā kriyate spaṣṭatārthataḥ  MAnuv tatra tārāthamūlatvaṃ sarvaśaśastrasya ceṣyate sarvatrānugatatvena pṛthagoṅkriyate khilaiḥ  MAnuv otatvavācī hyoṅkāro vaktayasau tadguṇotatām sa eva brahmaśabdārtho nārāyaṇapadoditaḥ  MAnuv sa eva bhargaśabdārtho vyāhṛtīnāṃ ca bhūmataḥ bhāvanāccaiva sutvācca so yaṃ puruṣa ityapi  MAnuv sa eva sarvavedārtho jijñāsyo yaṃ vidhīyate jñānī priyatamo to me taṃ vidvāneva cāmṛtaḥ  MAnuv vṛṇute yaṃ tena labhya ityādyuktibalena hi jijñāsotthajñānajāt tatprasādādeva mucyate  MAnuv dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvo jīva eva ca yadanugrahataḥ santi na santi yadupekṣayā  MAnuv narte tvat kriyate kiñcidityāderna hariṃ vinā jñānasvabhāvato pi syānmuktiḥ kasyāpi hi kvacit  MAnuv ajñānāṃ jñānado viṣṇurjñānināṃ mokṣadaśca saḥ ānandadaśca muktānāṃ sa evaiko janārdanaḥ  MAnuv ityukterbandhamithyātvaṃ naiva muktirapekṣate mithyātvamapi bandhasya na pratyakṣavirodhataḥ  MAnuv mithyātvaṃ yadi duḥkhādestadvākyāgrato bhavet mithyāyāḥ sādhakatvaṃ ca na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ  MAnuv tacca mithyāpramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā satā ced dvaitasiddhiḥ syānna siddhaṃ cānyasādhanam  MAnuv sādhakatvaṃ satastena sākṣiṇā siddhimicchatā svīkṛtaṃ hyaviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhakatā punaḥ  MAnuv taccāviśeṣamānena sādhyamityanavasthitiḥ anaṅgīkurvatāṃ viśvasatyatāṃ tanna vāditā  MAnuv tasmād vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satyetyeva vyavasthitā vyāvahārikametasmāt satyamityeva cāgatam  MAnuv vyavahārasataścāpi sādhakatvaṃ tu pūrvavat sattraividhyaṃ ca mānena siddhayet keneti pṛcchyate  MAnuv tasyāpyuktaprakāreṇa naiva siddhiḥ kathañcana vailakṣaṇyaṃ sadasatorapyetena niṣidhyate  MAnuv vailakṣaṇyaṃ sataścāpi svayaṃ sadbhedavādinaḥ asataścāpi viśvasya tenāniṣyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet  MAnuv yadyucyate pi sarvasmāditi sadbhedasaṃsthitiḥ sanmātratvaṃ brahmaṇo pi tasmāt tadapi no bhavet  MAnuv jñānabādhyatvamapi tu na siddhaṃ prativādinaḥ vijñātasyānyathā samyag vijñānaṃ hyeva tanmatam  MAnuv asadvilakṣaṇajñaptyai jñātavyamasadeva hi tasmādasatpratītiśca kathaṃ tena nivāryate  MAnuv anyathātvamasat tasmād bhrāntāveva pratīyate sattvasyāsata evaṃ hi svīkāryaiva pratītatā  MAnuv tasyānirvacanīyatve syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ nirviśeṣe svayaṃ bhāte kimajñānāvṛtaṃ bhavetaḥ  MAnuv mithyāviśeṣo pyajñānasiddhimeva hyapekṣate nacāavaraṇamajñānamasatye tena ceṣyate  MAnuv aprakāśasvarūpatvājjaḍe jñānaṃ na manyate ajñānābhāvataḥ śāstraṃ sarvaṃ vyarthībhaviṣyati  MAnuv ajñānasya ca mithyātvamajñānāditi kalpane anavasthitistathāca syādanyonyāśrayatāthavā  MAnuv svabhāvājñānavādasya nirdoṣatvānna tad bhavet avidyādurghaṭatvaṃ cet syādātmāpi hi tādṛśaḥ  MAnuv ato dhikāriviṣayaphalayogādivarjitam anantadoṣaduṣṭaṃ ca heyaṃ māyāmataṃ śubhaiḥ  MAnuv satyatvāt tena duḥkhādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ na brahmatāṃ vaded vedo jīvasya hi kathañcana  MAnuv yajamānaprastaratvaṃ yathā nārthaḥ śruterbhavet brahmatvamapi jīvasya pratyakṣasyāviśeṣataḥ  MAnuv sārvajñyādiguṇaṃ jīvād bhinnaṃ jñāpayati śrutiḥ īśaṃ tāmupajīvyaiva vartate hyaikyavādinī  MAnuv upajīvyavirodhena nāsyāstanmānatā bhavet svātantrye ca viśiṣṭatve sthānamattyaikyayorapi  MAnuv sādṛśye caikyavāk samyak sāvakāśā yatheṣyataḥ avakāśojkhitā bhedaśrutirnātibalā katham  MAnuv ajñānāsambhavādeva mithyābhedo nirākṛtaḥ ato yathārthabandhasya vinā viṣṇuprasādataḥ  MAnuv anivṛttestadarthaṃ hi jijñāsātra vidhīyate yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandhāpanodakṛt  MAnuv evaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryād bandhavibhedanam kāryatā ca na kācit syādiṣṭasādhanatāṃ vinā  MAnuv kāryaṃ na hi kriyāvyāpyaṃ niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ na bhaviṣyatkriyā kāryaṃ srakṣyatīśa iti hyapi  MAnuv kāryaṃ syānnaiva cākartumaśakyaṃ kāryamiṣyate sāmyādeva niṣiddhasya tadiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ tathā  MAnuv kāryaṃ sādhanamiṣṭasya bhagavāniṣṭadevatā mukhyeṣyaṃ vā sumanasāṃ preyastaditi ca śrutiḥ  MAnuv prāṇabuddhimanaḥkhātmadehāpatyadhanādayaḥ yatsamparkāt priyā āsaṃstataḥ ko nvaparaḥ priyaḥ  MAnuv ityādivākyairākāṅkṣāsannidhiryogyatā yataḥ asminneva samastasyetīṣye vyutpattiriṣyate  MAnuv attyapūpāṃstava bhrātetyādāvāvāpato pi ca udvāpād vartamānatvādākāṅkṣādibalādapi  MAnuv bālo vyutpattimapyeti nānayetyādivākyataḥ ānīyamānadṛṣṭayaiva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati  MAnuv eṣyadānayanāyāyaṃ kuta eva pratīkṣate vyutpanno vartamāne tu kriyāśabde bhaviṣyati  MAnuv punardṛṣṭyaiva śabdaśrut paścāt vyutpattimeṣyati vartamānamatītaṃ ca bhaviṣyaditi ca kramāt  MAnuv ākāṅkṣādiyutaṃ yasmād vidhervyutpādanaṃ kutaḥ dṛṣṭyā jñātapadārthasya padākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati  MAnuv vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmād vatarmāne gate tataḥ iṣṭamākāṅkṣate sarvo na pravṛttimapekṣate  MAnuv aparokṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā jñānamiṣṭasya sādhanam kvāpi ceṣyā tadarthā syādattirhi rasavittaye  MAnuv vākyārthajñānamātreṇa kvacidiṣṭaṃ bhavedapi na ca srukasruvavahnayādāvatātparyaṃ śruterbhavet  MAnuv yatkiñcitkaraṇarasyāpi yajñataivānyathā bhavet tasmādupāsanārthaṃ ca svārthe tātparyavad bhavet  MAnuv iti śabdonnaye gnāvityunnīte smṛtirbhavet itiśabdavyapetāni hyapi santi vacāṃsyalam  MAnuv ātmānamevetyādīni yoge gnāvapi tat samam ekavākyatvayoge tu vedasyāpi hyaśeṣataḥ  MAnuv vākyabhedo na yuktaḥ syād yogaśca syānmahāphale iti brūyāditi vaco gatamagnau samīpagam  MAnuv kalpanāgauravaṃ cet syāt pṛthak tātparyasambhave kalpanāgauravādeva padārthā na syureva hi  MAnuv pramāṇāvagatatvaṃ cet tātparyāṇaśaṃ tathaiva hi tasmāt padārthe vākyārthe tātparyamubhayatra ca  MAnuv pṛthageva ca vākyatvaṃ pṛthaganvayato bhavet avāntaratvād vākyānāṃ vākyabhedo na dūṣaṇam  MAnuv aṅgīkṛtatvādapi taiḥ padārthānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak kriyāpadenānvayasya vākyabhedāddhi dūṣaṇam  MAnuv pratyakṣādivirodhe to gauṇārthasyāpi sambhavāt atātparyaṃ padārthe pi na kalpyamavirodhataḥ  MAnuv ato jñānaphalānyeva karmāṇi jñānameva hi mukhyaprasādadaṃ viṣṇorjijñāsāyāśca tad bhavet  MAnuv kartavyā tena jijñāsā śrutiprāmāṇyayogataḥ pratyakṣavacca prāmāṇyaṃ svata evāgamasya hi  MAnuv anavasthānyathā hi syādaprāmāṇyaṃ tathānyataḥ mithyājñaptipralambhādestena vedavirodhi yat  MAnuv na mānamapi vedānāmaṅgīkāryā hi nityatā na hi dharmādisiddhiḥ syānnityavākyaṃ vinā kvacit  MAnuv avipralambhastajjñānaṃ tatkṛtatvādayo pi ca kalpyā gauravadoṣeṇa puṃvākyaṃ jñāpakaṃ na tat  MAnuv pratyakṣaḥ kasyacid dharmo vastutvāditi codite na buddho dharmadarśī syāt puṃstvādityanumāhatiḥ  MAnuv adharmavādino vākyamaprayojanameva hi dharmābhāvo pi no tena pratyakṣāvagato bhavet  MAnuv ataḥ saṃśayasampattau vākyaṃ pratyakṣavat pramā śaktiścaivānvite svārthe śabdānāmanubhūyate  MAnuv ato nvitābhidhāyitvaṃ gauravaṃ kalpane nyathā nacāśakyābhidhāyitvaṃ pravṛttiśca dvidhānyathā  MAnuv etat sarvaṃ tarkaśāstre brahmatarke hi vistarāt uktaṃ vidyāpṛthaktavāttu saṅkṣepeṇātra sūcitam  MAnuv pramāṇanyāyasacchikṣā kriyate tarkaśāstrataḥ mānanyāyaistu tatsiddhaimīmāṃsā meyaśodhanam  MAnuv brahmatarkaṃ ca bhagavān sa eva kṛtavān prabhuḥ pañcāśatkoṭivistārānnārāyaṇatanau kṛtāt  MAnuv uddhṛtya pañcasāhasraṃ kṛtavān bādarāyaṇaḥ atastadarthaṃ saṅkṣepādata ityabhyasūcayat  MAnuv yato nubhavataḥ sarvaṃ siddhametadato pi ca devaiśca durgamārtheṣu vyāpṛto nātivistṛtim  MAnuv cakāraitā hyavajñeyā yuktayaḥ pratipakṣagāḥ pratyakṣekṣākṣamaḥ pakṣaṃ kamevātrābhivīkṣate  MAnuv tasmādakṣamapakṣatvānmokṣaśāstre bhyupekṣitaḥ svayaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇurbrahmetyetat puroditam  MAnuv sa viṣṇurāha hīyante devaśāstrasya tena hi ādyantaṃ devaśāstrasya svayaṃ bhagavatā kṛtam  MAnuv madhyaṃ tadājñayā pailaśeṣābhyāṃ kṛtamañjasā atastatraiva viṣṇutvasiddherbrahmetyasūcayat  MAnuv doṣāracchidraśabdānāṃ paryāyatvaṃ yatastataḥ guṇā nārā iti jñeyastadvān nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  MAnuv brahmaśabdo pi hi guṇapūrtimeva vadatyayam ato nārāyaṇasyaiva jijñāsātra vidhīyate  MAnuv siddhatvād brahmaśabdasya viṣṇau spaṣṭatayā śrutau ambhasyapāra ityukto nārāyaṇapaderitaḥ  MAnuv āpo nārā iti hyāha sa evāpsvantarīritaḥ kāmato vidhirudrādipadadātṛyā svayaṃ śriyā  MAnuv yonitvenātmano viṣṇostiṣṭhantītyuditasya ca yasmin devā adhītyuktavā samudraṃ sthānameva ca  MAnuv nāma cākṣaramityeva ṛca ityuditaṃ tu yat yataḥ prasūtetyuktavā ca tadeva brahma cābravīt  MAnuv antaḥsamudragaṃ viśvaprasūteḥ kāraṇaṭha tu yat sūktopaniṣadādyuktaṃ janmādyasyeti lakṣyate  MAnuv sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhāro niyatirjñānamāvṛtiḥ bandhamokṣāvapi hyāsu śrutiṣūktā hareḥ sadā  MAnuv yaṃ nāmāni viśantyaddhā yo devānāmiti hyapi śruternāmāni sarvāṇi viṣṇoreva yatastataḥ  MAnuv ato na mukhyato nāma tadanyasya hi kasyacit guṇāḥ śrutā iti hyasmānna doṣo rthaḥ śruterbhavet  MAnuv prītyā mokṣaparatvācca tātparyaṃ naiva dūṣaṇe sarveṣāmapi vākyānāṃ mahātātparyamatra hi  MAnuv tadvirodhe na mānatvaṃ phalaṃ muktirhi vākyataḥ na purāṇādimānatvaṃ viruddhārthe śruterbhavet  MAnuv darśanāntaramūlatvānmohārthaṃ cājñayā hareḥ na sarvanāmatānyeṣāṃ śrutāvuktā hi kutracit  MAnuv adoṣavacanāccaiva niyamena hareḥ śrutau ajñānaṃ pāratantryaṃ ca praḷaye bhāva eva ca  MAnuv aśaktiścoditānyeṣāṃ sarveṣāmapi ca śrutau janmādyasyeti tenaitad viṣṇoreva svalakṣaṇam  MAnuv asyodbhavādihetutvaṃ sākṣādeva svalakṣaṇam kṛṣṇaddhayānacchalenaiva svayaṃ bhāgavate bravīt  MAnuv ato jīvaikyamapi sa nirācakre jagadguruḥ na hi janmādihetutvaṃ jīvasya jagato bhavet  MAnuv hitākriyādidoṣaṃ ca vakṣyatyeva svayaṃ prabhuḥ nirguṇatvaṃ ca tenaiva niṣiddhaṃ prabhuṇā svayam  MAnuv bhedenaiva tu mukhyārthasambhave lakṣaṇā kutaḥ kathaṃ nityaguṇasyāsya syādaikyaṃ guṇahānataḥ  MAnuv sadaiva guṇavattve sya bhinnaṃ syānnirguṇaṃ sadā na ca mithyāguṇatvaṃ syādanirvācyasya dūṣaṇāt  MAnuv nirguṇatvaṃ tadā ca syādāsuratvaṃ nacānyathā lakṣyalakṣaṇayorbhedo bhedo vā yadi vobhayam  MAnuv iti pṛṣṭe tadaikyasya gatireva na vidyate aikyābhede na śāstreṇa jñeyaṃ tat svaprakāśataḥ  MAnuv bhede mithyātvato bhedasatyatvaṃ syād balādapi bhedābhedau yadi tadā syādeva hyanavasthitiḥ  MAnuv svanirvāhakatā cet syād bāhyaṃ bāhakamityapi paryāyo bhedavān vā syādanavasthobhayatra ca  MAnuv satyajñānādike pyeva na vyāvṛttyā prayojanam vyāvṛttasyāviśeṣatve tadakhaṇḍaṃ ca khaṇḍitam nirviśeṣatvametena mūko hamitivad bhavet  MAnuv abhinne pi viśeṣo yaṃ balādāpatati hyataḥ viśeṣatadvatoścaiva svanirvāhakatā bhavet  MAnuv bhedahīne tvaparyāyaśabdāntaraniyāmakaḥ viśeṣo nāma kathitaḥ so sti vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ  MAnuv viśeṣāste pyanantāśca parasparaviśeṣiṇaḥ svanirvāhakatāyuktāḥ santi vastuṣvaśeṣataḥ  MAnuv ato nantaguṇaṃ brahma nirbhedamapi bhaṇyate evaṃ dharmāniti śrutyā tadabhedo pyudīryate  MAnuv śaivādyāgamasamprāptadṛṣṭagena phalena tu tadvākyopamayānyacca pramāṇatve numīyate  MAnuv īśavākyatvata iti cet tadgavyabhicāriṇā aprāmāṇyānumā ca syānna pṛthak cānumeśvare  MAnuv puṃstvahetubalādeva pūrvoktenaiva vartmanā śāstrayonitvametena kāraṇasya balād bhavet  MAnuv nāvedavinna tarkeṇa matirityādivākyataḥ tarko jñāpayituṃ śakto neśitāraṃ kathañcana  MAnuv vanakṛttvādirūpeṇa pakṣabhūtasya ceśituḥ kiñcijjñānaṃ hi puṃstvena śakyaṃ sādhayituṃ sukham  MAnuv vṛkṣakṛnnākhilaṃ vṛkṣaṃ vetti puṃstvāddhi caitravat ityādyanumayā spardhi nānumānaṃ pareśituḥ śaktaṃ vijñāpane cātiprasaṅgo numayedṛśā  MAnuv vastutvāt turagaḥ śṛṅgī puṣpavat khaṃ sutairyutā citriṇī ca rasaḥ ṣaṣṭho rasatvāt sottaro bhavet upakramādiliṅgebhyo nānyāsyādanumā tataḥ  MAnuv ta evānvayanāmānastaiḥ samyak pravicārite mukhyārtho bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvaśāstrasya nāparaḥ  MAnuv īkṣaṇīyatvato viṣṇurvācya eva nacānyathā lakṣyatvaṃ kvāpi dṛṣṭaṃ hi kiṃ tadityanavasthitiḥ  MAnuv mādhuryādiviśeṣāśca tacchabdairuditāḥ sadā vākyārtho pi hi vākyārthaśabdenaivodito bhavet  MAnuv nāvācyaṃ tena kiñcit syād yata ityādikairvadan avācyatvaṃ kathaṃ brūyānmūko hamitivat sudhīḥ  MAnuv yena lakṣyamiti proktaṃ lakṣyaśabdena so vadat ekasyāpi hi śabdasya gauṇārthasvīkṛtau satām  MAnuv mahatī jāyate lajjā yatra tatrākhilā ravāḥ amukhyārthā iti vadan yastanmārgānuvartinām kathaṃ na jāyate lajjā vaktuṃ śābdatvamātmanaḥ  MAnuv ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāḥ sākṣāt pūrṇābhidhāyinaḥ janmādikāraṇaṃ brahma lakṣitaṃ ca yadā tadā  MAnuv vandhyāputropamaṃ māyāśabalaṃ vācyamityapi kalpayitvā vinā mānaṃ lakṣyaṃ śuddhaṃ vadan padaiḥ  MAnuv ātmaśabdoditasyaiva jñānaṃ muktāvasādhanam āha śrutaparityāgaḥ syāccāsyāśrutakalpanam  MAnuv syāt sarvatra ca yatraikamapi loko jugupsate niyamenobhayaṃ syāddhi yasya svaparayormate  MAnuv alaṅkṛtaḥ sadaivāyaṃ durghaṭaireva bhūṣaṇaiḥ andhantamo nityuduḥkhaṃ tasya syād vasanadvayam  MAnuv anandā nāma te lokā andhena tamasāvṛtāḥ tāṃste pretyābhigacchantyavidvāṃso budho janāḥ  MAnuv asuryā nāma te lokā andhena tamasāvṛtāḥ tāṃste pretyābhigacchanti ye kecātmahano janāḥ  MAnuv ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ śataśo tra samantataḥ heyatvāvacanāccaiva nātmā gauṇaḥ śrutau śrutaḥ  MAnuv tamevaikaṃ jānathānyā vāco muñcatha ceti ha ukta ātmā kathaṃ gauṇo heyapakṣe hyasau śrutaḥ  MAnuv parivāratayā grāhyā api heyāḥ pradhānataḥ pūrṇasya pūrṇamādāya pūrṇamevāvaśiṣyate  MAnuv iti svasyaiva pūrṇasya pūrṇe pyaya udāhṛtaḥ kathaṃ māyāvyavacchinnaḥ pūrṇo mukhyatayā bhavet  MAnuv padaṃ ca nirguṇa iti kathaṃ gauṇaṃ vadiṣyati guṇābhāvopalakṣyaṃ cet padaṃ tadapi vācakam  MAnuv ato navasthitimukhasarvadoṣamahāspadam kathametanmataṃ sadbhirādriyeta vicakṣaṇaiḥ  MAnuv na ca sāṅkhayanirākṛtyai sūtrāṇyetānyacīkḷpat bhagavān nahyaśabdatvaṃ pradhāne ṅgīkarotyasau  MAnuv samanvaye pratijñāte śabdagocarataiva hi prathamapratipādyā syāt tadabhāve kuto nvayaḥ  MAnuv kathaṃ ca lakṣaṇāvādī brūyād brahmasamanvayam yo sau śabdasya mukhyārthastatraiva syāt samanvayaḥ  MAnuv janmādikāraṇe sākṣādāha devaḥ samanvayam uktaṃ tadeva jijñāsyaṃ kvāvakāśo tra nirguṇe  MAnuv kathañcāsambhavastasya mukhyārthasya nirākṛtau mānena kena vijñeyamavācyājñeyanirguṇam  MAnuv ameyaṃ cenna śāstrasya tatra vṛttiḥ kathañcana tasmācchāstreṇa jijñāsyamasmadīyaṃ guṇārṇavam  MAnuv vāsudevākhyamadvandvaṃ paraṃ brahmākhilottamam vijñeyavācyalakṣyatvapūrvāśeṣaviśeṣataḥ  MAnuv nirgataṃ manaso vāco yadi tat syādagocaram astu tanmā vaded vādī nacāsmacchāstragaṃ tu tat  MAnuv avācyaṃ vācyamityuktavā kimityunmattavanmṛṣā asmacchāstrasya cauryāya yatate svoktidūṣakaḥ  MAnuv janmādikāraṇaṃ yattat sākṣānnārāyaṇābhidham vadantu śrutayo brahma śāstraṃ caitat tadarthataḥ  MAnuv svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā  MAnuvpravṛttamastvavācyaṃ te maiva brūyāḥ kathañcana sarvaśabdairavācyaṃ taduktavā tadviṣayaṃ punaḥ  MAnuv vayaṃ tvāṃ śrutiyuktibhyāṃ baddhvāsmacchāstramañjasā vicārayāmaḥ śrutibhiryuktibhiścaiva sādaram  MAnuv adbhutatvādavācyaṃ tadatarkyājñeyameva ca anantaguṇapūrṇatvādityūde paiṅgināṃ śrutiḥ avācyamiti loke pi vaktayāścāryatamaṃ bhuvi  MAnuv evaṃ śāstrāvagamyatve vibhāgena samanvayam ānandamaya ityādinādhyāyena vadatyajaḥ  MAnuv tatrānyatra prasiddhānāṃ viṣṇāveva samanvayam śabdānāṃ prathame pāde guṇisāmānyavācinām  MAnuv guṇavācināṃ ca prathamamāha devaḥ samanvayam samudraśāyinaṃ sarvaprasūtiprasavaṃ śrutiḥ  MAnuv tadeva brahma paramamiti sāvadhṛtirjagau yato to brahmaśabdasya tatraiva niyatatvataḥ  MAnuv yo nnaṃ brahmetyādirūpādabhyāsāt taittirīyake anyāsu caitadrūpāsu śākhāsvapi sahasraśaḥ  MAnuv ānandamaya ityādyaiḥ śabdairvācyo hariḥ svayam upalakṣaṇatvaṃ śabdānāmānandamayapūrviṇām  MAnuv sūtrasyālpākṣaratvena sarvaśākhāvinirṇaye punaśca prāpakāddhetostatrādhikaraṇāntaram  MAnuv sarve vedā āmananti yat padaṃ svataḥ yathaiva kṛṣṇakeśasya kṛṣṇasya brahmatākhilā  MAnuv darśitā caiva pārthāya niḥsīmāḥ śaktayo sya hi ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam  MAnuv viṣṇvākhyamuktamanyatra hyūrdhvaretaṃ ca hyeva śrutyartho vasito bhavet  MAnuv ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma prati viṣṇuṃ sadāśivaḥ ūrdhvaretā dhyāyati ha śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ  MAnuv ityarthametamevāha nīlagrīvaśrutiḥ parā ārtharvaṇī paraṃ brahma tasmādeko hariḥ śrutau  MAnuv tadevartamiti prāha kathamevānyathā śrutiḥ avadhārayantī tasyaiva hyṛtatvādikamañjasā  MAnuv eko nārāyaṇa āsīnna brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ vāsudevo gra evāsīnna brahmā na ca duḥkhaṃ syādataḥ kevalalīlayā pravartako na cedeṣa prāṇyādanyācca kaḥ pumān  MAnuv brahmavit paramāpnotīti yat prathamasūcitam tadeva mantravarṇena satyaṃ jñānamanantavat  MAnuv lakṣitaṃ tatra manuṣyāḥ paśavaśca ye āyuḥ prāṇo hi bhūtānāmiti yad gatijīvane  MAnuv ukte saditidhātvartho gatiścāto hi satyatā prāṇatvamavabodhārtho manudhātuḥ prakīrtitaḥ  MAnuv nālpe sukhamiti balajñānasvarūpatvād vāyuragniragaṃ nayan  MAnuv āpa āpālanāccaiva pṛthivī prathito yataḥ uṣyānāmāśrayatvena sa evoṣadhināmakaḥ  MAnuv oṣadhīṣu sthito viṣṇuḥ kṣudhitairāśrito bhavet puri śete yataḥ so harimeva tu  MAnuv parāmṛśati tasyaiva pañcarūpatvavittaye tyaktavā bhūtādikaṃ sarvaṃ sa vā eṣa iti śrutiḥ  MAnuv sa ityātmapadoddiṣṭa eṣa jīvaśarīragaḥ sārānnamaya evāyaṃ na lokānnamayaḥ prabhuḥ  MAnuv iti taṃ rasaśabdena viśinaṣṭi śarīragam idamityeva nirdeśo vastraprāvṛtavad vibhoḥ  MAnuv śira āderbhavejjīvaśira ādau vyavasthiteḥ taṃ viditvāsya muktiḥ syānnānyajñānāt kathañcana  MAnuv āditye MAnuv bhāvābhāvasvarūpāstu viśeṣā eva vastunaḥ abhinnā eva saṅgrāhyā vyavahāraprasiddhaye  MAnuv yathaikaḥ samavāyo pi bhedābhedau ca vastuni aṅgīkāryā viśeṣeṇa sthāneṣu vyavahartṛbhiḥ  MAnuv payo mbvādi ca nopamā  MAnuv etatpraśāstivacanāccetanācetanasya ca dvaividhye pitu kāmādeḥ kutaḥ svāmitvamātmanaḥ  MAnuv sākṣādanubhavārūḍhaṃ śakyate podituṃ kvacit icchāsvāmitvamevoktamicchāvattvaṃ nacāparam  MAnuv kiñcit tadvaśagatve pi svāmitvaṃ lokavad bhavet sarvātmatantrakāmādeḥ kimutaiva pareśituḥ  MAnuv na cānubhavagaṃ kāmasvāmitvaṃ vedavāgapi śaktāpavadituṃ tasmāt sā tadanyābhidhāyinī  MAnuv mokṣakāmo bhavedanyo yadi muktād bhaviṣyataḥ mokṣakāmasya kiṃ tena svanāśārthaṃ ca ko yatet  MAnuv kartṛtvaṃ yasya tasyaiva bhoktṛtvamupalabhyate vibhāge ca tayormānaṃ naiva kiñcit kvacid bhavet  MAnuv sarvamānavirodhaikadurdīkṣādīkṣitastvayam māyāvādyupamāṃ yāyāt taccaśabdānnirākṛtaḥ  MAnuv sāṅkhayastu seśvaro brūte kṣetrānugrahaśaktimān astīśvaraḥ svayambhātaḥ kleśakarmādivarjitaḥ  MAnuv kṣetraśaktimatī saiva prakṛtirbījaśaktimān jīvaḥ parjanyavad daivaśaktimānīśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ  MAnuv pṛthivīvat pradhānaṃ tajjīvaḥ sannidhimātrataḥ bījāvapanakartevetyatra prāha prabhuḥ svayam  MAnuv anyatra kāpi śaktirna svātantryeṇeśa eva hi śaktīstāḥ prerayatyañjastadadhīnāśca sarvadā  MAnuv sattāpradhānapuruṣaśaktīnāṃ ca pratītayaḥ pravṛttayaśca tāḥ sarvā nityaṃ nityātmanā yataḥ  MAnuv yathā nityatayā nityaṃ nityaśaktayā svayeśvaraḥ niyāmayati nityaṃ ca na ṛte tvaditi śruteḥ  MAnuv svabhāvajīvakarmāṇi dravyaṃ kālaḥ śrutiḥ kriyāḥ yatprasādādime santi na santi yadupekṣayā  MAnuv iti śruterna sattādyā api nārāyaṇaṃ vinā tatpatañjalivindhyādimataṃ na puruṣārthadam  MAnuv cārvākairucyate mānamakṣajaṃ nāparaṃ kvacit deha ātmā pumarthaśca kāmārthābhyāṃ vinā na hi  MAnuv yadevaṃ darśanenāsya ko rthaḥ pratyakṣagocaraḥ labdhastenaiva hi naraiḥ śāstrāt kiṃ mohanaṃ vinā  MAnuv svaparārthavihīnatvāt svamatenaiva niṣphalam kimityunmattavacchāstraṃ vṛthā pralapati svayam  MAnuv dehādanyo nubhavata ātmā bhāti śarīriṇām mama deha iti vyaktaṃ mamārtha itivat sadā  MAnuv pratyakṣasyaiva mānatvamiti kenāvasīyate yadi tatsādhakaṃ vedaprāmāṇye na kathaṃ bhavet  MAnuv na cānyāmānatā kvāpi pramāṇenāvasīyate svamatenārtharahita upekṣyaḥ pakṣa īdṛśaḥ  MAnuv sannidhānāccetanasya vartate yadyacetanam tathāpyabuddhipūrvatvāduktadoṣaḥ samo bhavet  MAnuv aṅgitvaṃ puruṣasyaiva sarvairapyanubhūyate tadaṅgatvoktitaścaiva syāt sarvasyāpalāpakaḥ kimu sarveśvarasyāsya hyapalāṣād yato khilam  MAnuv aṅgitvaṃ yadi tasyaiva svātantryaṃ cennacākhilam tatpreraṇe pyaśaktatvāt svatantro nyo hyapekṣitaḥ  MAnuv na ca svātantryamasyaiva pratyakṣādivirodhataḥ hitākṛtyādidoṣācca bhadraṃ nānīśvaraṃ matam  MAnuv saṃsāriṇo nyaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvaśaktimanaupamam cetanācetanasyāsya sattvādestadadhīnatām nāṅgīkurvanti ye teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca samā ime  MAnuv tasmācchrutipramāṇena yuktibhiśca paro hariḥ aṅgīkāyartamo nityaḥ sarvairapi suniścitam  MAnuv nityajñānaprayatnecchaṃ saṅkhayadyairapi pañcabhiḥ yuktamīśaṃ vadantyanye tadicchādṛṣṭacoditāḥ paramāṇavaścaturvargāḥ saṃyujyante dviśo khilāḥ  MAnuv paramāṇudvayenaiva dvayaṇukaṃ nāma jāyate dvayaṇukatrayeṇa tṛyaṇukaṃ taiścaturbhistadātmakam  MAnuv tatastvaniyamenaiva khaṇḍāvayavināṃ bhavaḥ tataścāniyamenaiva sarvāvayavisambhavaḥ  MAnuv kāraṇaṃ samavāyyākhyaṃ paramāṇvādi tatra hi īśecchādṛṣṭakālāstu nimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ matam  MAnuv sāmānyāntyaviśeṣau ca samavāyaśca tattrayam nityaṃ kriyā anityāstu guṇadravye dvirūpake  MAnuv kārye guṇakriyāṇāṃ tu samavāyyanyakāraṇam kāraṇasthā guṇādyāstu saṃyogo dravyakāraṇam  MAnuv evaṃ sthite pi siddhānte viśeṣastatra kalpitaḥ dvayaṇuke paramāṇau ca hrasvatvaṃ parimaṇḍalam  MAnuv na kāraṇaṃ kāryaguṇe vairūpyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ityāhustānathovāca vidyādhīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ  MAnuv mahattvaṃ caiva dīrghatvaṃ tṛyaṇukādyeṣu kalpitam tasmācca sadṛśaṃ kāryaṃ tatkāryeṣūpajāyate  MAnuv yathā tathaiva hrasvatvāt pārimāṇḍalyato pi hi jāyeta sadṛśaṃ kārye parimāṇaṃ samatvataḥ  MAnuv na cenmahattvataścaiva dīghartvādapi no bhavet sadṛśasya hi kāryasya naiva yogaḥ kathañcana  MAnuv apratyakṣatvamevaṃ syād yataḥ kāryeṣvaṇutvataḥ iti cenna mahattvaṃ ca paramāṇāvaṇāvapi kathaṃ tṛyaṇukapūrveṣu nāṇutvamapi kathyate  MAnuv pratyakṣatvatadanyatve puruṣāpekṣayākhile aṇutvaṃ ca mahattvaṃ ca yato vastuvyapekṣayā  MAnuv tāratamyasthitā yasmāt padārthāḥ sarva eva ca yathā mahattvaviśrāntistathāṇutvasya ceṣyate  MAnuv parimāṇatvataścenna mahattvasyāpi viśramaḥ dṛśyate nanta ityeva tathānantyamaṇāvapi  MAnuv na mahattatvaguṇata etāvāniti hīśvaraḥ paricchinnastathāṇośca naitāvadbhāgatā kvacit  MAnuv viśrānto yadyanantāṃśaḥ kaścidastīti gamyate nāvasāyayituṃ śakyo virodhādeva kevalam  MAnuv kevalaṃ sākṣimānena kālo deśo pi nāntavān aparyavasitiścāṇordṛśyate sakṣiṇā dvayoḥ  MAnuv yadi no sākṣigamyaṃ tanmahattvaṃ kena gamyate viśrāntistāratamyena dṛśyate hyanumānataḥ  MAnuv yadyāgamādanantaṃ tanmahattvamavagamyate anantameva cāṇutvaṃ kuto naivāvasīyate  MAnuv mahattvāṇutvayornaiva viśrāntirupalabhyate anyadeva hyanantatvaṃ mahattvāṇutvayoḥ samam  MAnuv bahutvālpatvayoryadvat sāṅkhayāyāmupalabhyate ānantyamekabhāgānāṃ tāvattvaṃ hyeva gaṇyate  MAnuv aṇīyāṃśca mahīyāṃśca bhagavānāgamoditaḥ ānantyavācakaḥ śabdo dvidhānantye pi mānatām  MAnuv yāti naiva guṇālpatvaṃ kālātpatvaṃ ca mānagam sarvakālagatasyālpakāle pi syādavasthitiḥ  MAnuv mahāguṇasya cālpo pi guṇaḥ syāditi ced bhavet tāvattvameva naiva syād deśe pyetanna no matam  MAnuv mahato lpatvamapi hi vyomavat prāha vedavit yadyalpadeśasaṃsthānaṃ na sarvatrāpi no bhavet  MAnuv sthitasya hyalpadeśeṣu sarvagatvaṃ bhaved dhruvam ekatrāpyanavasthasya kuta evākhilasthatā  MAnuv śūnyatvameva tasya syād yasyaikatrāpi na sthitiḥ ato nāṇutvaviśrāntirna mahattvasya ca kvacit  MAnuv ubhayānantyayuk tasmād yadi mukhyamahad bhavet tacca brahma paraṃ sākṣāt sarvānantyayutaṃ sadā  MAnuv yadi sākṣī svayambhāto na mānaṃ kena gamyate akṣajādeśca mānatvamanavasthāthavā bhavet  MAnuv ataḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ bhāgāḥ santyeva sarvadā sarvadikṣvapi sambandhādavibhāgaḥ parāṇutā  MAnuv tatsaṃyogādaniyatāt padārthānāṃ janirbhavet dvayoreva tu saṃyoga iti kenāvasīyate  MAnuv kāraṇasya guṇāstena bhaveyuḥ kāryagā api tāratamyena sarve pi mahāntaścāṇavo yataḥ  MAnuv na ca tatproktasṛṣṭau tu mānaṃ kevalakalpanā kathaṃ sākṣimitasyāsya śaknuyād vāraṇe kvacit  MAnuv yadi sākṣimitaṃ naitannānumā tatra vartate pakṣīkartumaśakyatvāt kuta evānumā bhavet  MAnuv yatra nāsti padanyāsaḥ kastaṃ viṣayamāpnuyāt deśāntarādiśabdaśca śaśaśṛṅgādiśabdavat  MAnuv sadṛśaṃ ca sajātīyaṃ nāsmatpakṣe kim eva hi yenaiva ca prakāreṇātyasiddhamanumīyate tenaiva śaśṛṅgādeḥ śakyamastitvakalpanam  MAnuv pratyakṣamāgamo vāpi bhaved yatra niyāmakaḥ saiva vyāptirbhavenmānaṃ nānyā sandigdhamūlataḥ  MAnuv sahadarśanamātreṇa na vyāptiravasīyate yadaivāvyatirekasya hyakṣajaṃ vāgamo bhavet tannirdhāritayuktirvā vyāptiḥ saivāparā na hi  MAnuv anyathā saptamarasabhavo pyanumayāpatet aniṣṭāni ca sarvāṇi hyanumā kāmacāriṇī  MAnuv kāryakāraṇayoścaiva guṇādeḥ pañcakasya ca bhinnasyaiva tu sambandhaḥ samavāyo nya īryate  MAnuv bhinnatvasāmyatastasya tābhyāṃ yogo bhaved dhruvam sa svanirvāhakaścet syād dravyameva tathā na kim  MAnuv viśeṣastadgatatvādiryadyabhinne vasīyate guṇakriyādirūpasya niṣedhaḥ kena hetunā  MAnuv dravyameva tato nantaviśeṣātmatayā sadā nānāvyavahṛterheturanantatvaṃ viśeṣataḥ  MAnuv viśeṣaśca viśeṣī saḥ svenaiva samavāyavat kalpanāgurutādoṣāt padārthāntaratā na hi  MAnuv kalpayitvā ṣaṭ padārthān sābhāvānapi kevalam ekasmin sa viśeṣaścet kiṃ pūrvaṃ tasya vismṛtiḥ  MAnuv yena pratyakṣasiddhena vyavahāro khilo bhavet bhāvābhāvavibhāgena yaṃ vinā na kathañcana  MAnuv abhedena pratītiśca kāryakāraṇapūrvake abhāvānte padārthe smin saviśeṣāvasīyate  MAnuv sāmānyādipadārtheṣu tanniṣṭhatvādayo khilāḥ kathaṃ dharmā nivāryante vastvaikye pi hi vādibhiḥ  MAnuv kāryasya tattanniṣṭhatvaṃ guṇādervyāpitādikaḥ kathaṃ viśeṣo naivāsti sa ca dharmo paro yadi  MAnuv ṣaṭpadārthātirekaḥ syāt padārthāniyame pi hi dharmasya dharmasantānādanavasthākaro bhavet  MAnuv sāmānyasyāpi sāmānyaṃ guṇasyāpi guṇo hyataḥ nāṅgīkṛtaḥ sa ca yadi nānavasthā kvacid bhavet  MAnuv asmatpakṣe guṇādyāśca tadvanto hi viśeṣataḥ ananyatvānnānavasthā bhedo nāśe bhavet tathā  MAnuv viśeṣameva saṃśritya viśeṣo balavān yataḥ dṛṣṭipramāṇataścaiva virodho darśane katham  MAnuv virodho hyavirodhaśca yato darśanamānagau tato dṛṣṭe virodhastu sadbhirāpādyate katham  MAnuv abhinno bhagavān svena tadanyena vibhedavān nityā dharmāstadīyāstu sarve smānnaiva bhedinaḥ  MAnuv sāmastyocchedino nyatra dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ bhāve ta eva cocchedāt tadanye ca samastaśaḥ  MAnuv aṃśāṃśinorabhedena tvaṃśasaṃyoga eva hi aṃśino nānavasthāto yadyapyaṃśeṣvaviśramaḥ  MAnuv ekasmin jāta evānyaḥ saṃyogo jāyate yadi anavasthā tadaiva syāt saṃyogaikye bhavet kva sā  MAnuv aṃśe saṃyogadṛṣṭeśca dṛṣṭe kā sānavasthitiḥ yadyaṃśago na saṃyogaḥ kāryeṣu prathimā katham  MAnuv paramāṇoraṇornāsti mahattetyadbhutaṃ vacaḥ aṇūnāṃ prathimāpekṣāṃ vinaiva tṛyaṇuke pi saḥ paramāṇormahattvaṃ ca vinetyetad vacaḥ katham  MAnuv aṃśino ṃśairabhedo yamaṃśena tu bhidābhidā sarvapratyakṣaviṣayaḥ kathameva hyapohyate  MAnuv saṃyogaśca vibhāgaśca bhedaścaiva pṛthak pṛthak anyonyapratiyogena hyubhayorapi dṛśyate  MAnuv bhinnā iti tu bhedānāṃ samudāyo hi dṛśyate yathaiva ca padārthānāmanayorbheda ityapi  MAnuv ito muṣyāmuto pyasya bhedo dṛṣṭo dvidharmikaḥ tatraikavacanaṃ yattad viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ yathā  MAnuv naratvādikamapyevaṃ tattaddharmatayeyate na sarvadharma eko sti samudāyastu bhinnagaḥ  MAnuv etādṛśaṃ ca sādṛśyaṃ padārtheṣu pṛthak pṛthak ekasmin sa vinaṣṭe pi yato nyatraiva dṛśyate  MAnuv kuto bhasmatvamāptasya naratvaṃ punariṣyate ekatve nāsti mānaṃ ca śrutirapyāha sādaram  MAnuv bhinnāśca bhinnadharmāśca padārthā akhilā api svaiḥ svairdharmairabhinnāśca svarūpairapi sarvaśaḥ  MAnuv anivṛttavināśāstu dharmā ubhayarūpakāḥ na kenacidabhinno to bhagavān svaguṇairvinā  MAnuv iti vyutpattirapi hi sādṛśyenaiva gamyate sarveṣu yugapacchabdaḥ sadṛśeṣu pravartate  MAnuv tathāpi prāptitastvekavacanācca viśeṣataḥ abhīṣyāvagatiśca syācchaktiḥ sādṛśyagā yataḥ  MAnuv tādṛśo yaṃ ca tacchabda iti jñāpayati sphuṭam jātitaścet kathaṃ tāsu tatra cedanavasthitiḥ  MAnuv tathaiva vyaktivijñānaṃ vyaktitvābhāvadūṣitam yadi taccāsti tasyāpi viśeṣeṣvanavasthitiḥ  MAnuv kathaṃ svarūpatvamapi jñāyate nugataṃ yadi ekavyutpattiparyantamanavasthādidūṣitam kalpanāgauravāt tena yuktā nānugakalpanā  MAnuv aupādhikaviśiṣṭādyamapi tadvastu kiṃ tataḥ anyat tadeva cedagnimattvaṃ kiṃ tatra bhaṇyate  MAnuv agnisaṃyogamātraṃ ced bhavet tat siddhasādhanam bhūdharasyāgnisaṃyogo yadi ṣaṣṭhayartha eva kaḥ  MAnuv samavāyo yadi hy asya caikatvāt siddhasādhanam yadyasyaupādhiko bhedaḥ kuta ekatvamiṣyate  MAnuv nānirvācyaṃ hi teneṣyamata aupādhikānyayoḥ satyatvāt ko viśeṣaḥ syānmāyāvādyanyathā bhavet  MAnuv upādhijanyaṃ tadgamyamiti vaupādhikaṃ bhavet ubhayatrāpyanantāḥ syuḥ samavāyā itastataḥ bhinnatvaṃ caiva teṣvasti ko viśeṣa upādhige  MAnuv avidyamāna evānyaḥ samavāyo dhigamyate upādhinā tadgamakamanumānaṃ na mā bhavet  MAnuv evamevāsataḥ sattasamavāyo janirmatā tatrāpi hyuktadoṣāṇāṃ naiva kiñcinnivārakam  MAnuv asmatpakṣe viśeṣasya sarvatrāṅgīkṛtatvataḥ nāsti doṣaḥ kvacid bhāvo hyabhāvaśca sa eva hi  MAnuv abhāvasya ca dharmāḥ syurbhāvāsteṣāṃ ca te khilāḥ pratyakṣamānataḥ sarvametanno vāraṇakṣamam sarve bhāvā abhāvāśca padārthāstena sarvadā  MAnuv tathāpi prathamaṃ buddheryo niṣedhasya gocaraḥ so bhāvo vidhibuddhestu gocaraḥ prathamaṃ paraḥ  MAnuv tasmāt pradhvastabhedādi sadityevāvagamyate astyabhāvo sti ca dhvaṃso dehābhāvaśca bhasmatā  MAnuv ityādi yujyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣādipramāṇataḥ anyonyābhāvabhedau ca pṛthaktavaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak  MAnuv yat kalpayanti taccaiva kalpanāgauravād gatam paryāyatvena te śabdā jñāyante sarva eva hi  MAnuv bhedasya tu svarūpatve ye vadanti ca śūnyatām adbhutatāste yato nyasya pratiyogitvamiṣyate  MAnuv pratiyogino hi bhedo yaṃ natu svasmāt kathañcana vibhāgenālpataiva syāt kuta eva ca śūnyatā  MAnuv na śūnyānāṃ hi saṃyogād bhāvo vastuna iṣyate vidāraṇārtho dhātuśca vibhāgaguṇavācakaḥ  MAnuv avidāraṇe pi hyāsyasya bhinnāvoṣṭhau tu tasya ca ata unmattavākyatvānmāyāvādo bhyupekṣitaḥ  MAnuv na cāmandasadānandasyandyanantaguṇārṇavaḥ īśvaro ṣṭaguṇatvena prameyo pramitatvataḥ  MAnuv mayyanantaguṇe nante guṇato nantavigrahe anantaguṇamāhātmyaśaktijñānamahārṇavaḥ  MAnuv nārāyaṇaḥ paro śeṣacetanebhyaḥ paraṃ padam ityādivedatadvākyairanantaiścāvasīyate  MAnuv anantaguṇatā viṣṇoḥ kathameva hyapodyate yadyanantaviśeṣāśca tajjñānādernivāritāḥ  MAnuv kathaṃ tattadviṣayatā sārvajñyārthaṃ vidhīyate aupādhikaviśeṣastu pūrvameva nirākṛtaḥ  MAnuv svaprakāśatvamapi tu yairjñānasya nivāritam kathaṃ sarvajñatā tasya svajñānādhigamaṃ vinā  MAnuv jñānaṃ viśvādhigaṃ tvekaṃ tajjñānaviṣayaṃ param iti jñānadvayenaiva sarvavit parameśvaraḥ  MAnuv iti cedeṣa evārthastajjñānāvasito yadi svaprakāśatvameva syājjñānaṃ hyetad viśeṣaṇam  MAnuv jñānāntareṇa cedatra bhavedevānavasthitiḥ svaprakāśatvametasmād durnivāryaṃ samāpatet  MAnuv sukhavān duḥkhavāṃśca syāditi vyāptiśca no bhavet nirduḥkhatvaṃ mahānandaḥ śrutyaiveśasya bhaṇyate  MAnuv yo śanāyāpipāse ca śokādīṃścātivartate ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān vipāpmetyādikā ca sā  MAnuv īśvarasya tatheṣṭatvaṃ duḥkhitvopādhirityapi ukte kimuttaraṃ brūyācchrutyanādaratatparaḥ  MAnuv nacātmaduḥkhitecchā syādata etannivāryate sahadarśanamātreṇa śrutīnāmapalāpakaḥ  MAnuv yajñāder api pāpasya hetutvaṃ hiṃsayā yuteḥ nānumāti kathaṃ tatra yadyupādhirniṣiddhatā  MAnuv aduḥkhitvena cānuktiḥ kathaṃ nopādhitāṃ vrajet aduḥkhamitarat sarvaṃ jīvā eva tu duḥkhinaḥ teṣāṃ duḥkhaprahāṇāya śrutireṣā pravartate  MAnuv iti śrutirhi paramā śrutyuktir yadi kāraṇam kiṃ kāryamanumānena gaḷastanasamena hi  MAnuv anumānena yadyarthaḥ śrutidṛṣṭo vyapodyate pūrvoktena prakāreṇa neśvaro dharma eva MAnuv guṇasāmyamayogaśca tarkabādho vilomatā nānābhāvaḥ pralobhaśca pūrvapakṣagāḥ  MAnuv aśakyakartṛtāśaktiḥ svato bodhastadeva ca amānakḷptisanmānavyavasthātyalpatābhavāḥ  MAnuv viśeṣadṛṣṭivākye ca udbhāvanīyameva syānna kathāvasitirbhavet  MAnuv vijigīṣukathāyāṃ tu kathāvasitikāraṇam parihāre pi siddhatvaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ pratijñāyāṃ tadanyasya siddhataiva hi sādhakā  MAnuv āśrayavyāśrayāsiddhī sādhyasiddhiśca dūṣaṇam keṣāñcin na ca te doṣā vyāptau satyāṃ kathañcana  MAnuv doṣo vyāhatirevāsti nṛśṛṅgāstitvasādhane yatra vyāhatatā nāsti ko tisaṅgo sya sādhane  MAnuv bhojanādīnāmiṣṭasādhanatānumā mānaṃ vyavahṛtau nityaṃ vyabhicāro hi tatra ca  MAnuv vyāptatve vyāśrayatvaṃ tu kathameva hi dūṣaṇam rohiṇyudaya āsannaḥ kṛttikābhyuditā yataḥ ityukte sādhanaṃ no kiṃ na hyājñaivātra sādhakā  MAnuv anyat sadasatorviśvamiti ca vyāhateramā asiddhasādhane doṣaḥ ko vyāptiryadi vidyate  MAnuv vyāptiśca vyatirekeṇa tatra taiścaiva gamyate aprasiddhasya sādhyasya sādhakatvaṃ yadeṣyate liṅgasyoktau viśeṣo yaṃ kena mānena gamyate  MAnuv sādhanaṃ paramāṇvāderyadāsiddhasya ceṣyate yathānubhavamevaitannāṅgīkāryaṃ kutastadā  MAnuv yatra nātiprasaṅgo sti mānaṃ na ca viparyate kliṣṭakalpanayaivātra sādhyamityatidurvacaḥ  MAnuv pariśeṣo mithaḥsiddhiḥ cakrakasvāśrayādayaḥ asiddhasādhakatvena pañcāvayavatāṃ vinā aṅgīkāryāḥ samastaistanniyamaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ  MAnuv siddasādhanatāyāṃ ca na kathāvasitirbhavet vyabhicāro hetvasiddhirekapakṣe pi dūṣaṇam  MAnuv sādhyasādhanavaikalyaṃ dṛṣṭāntasya viśeṣaṇe vaiyathyarmekāsiddhau ca viśiṣṭāsiddhireva hi  MAnuv aprayojakatā tatra prathamapraśnadūṣaṇam siddhapraśnādikaṃ yat tadādhikyāntagartaṃ bhavet  MAnuv arthāpattyupamābhāvā anumāntargatāḥ kvacit pratyakṣāntargato bhāvaḥ sukhāderniyamena ca  MAnuv anyatra khaḍiti prāptaḥ prārambhādyāśca yuktayaḥ āgamārthāvasityarthā niyatavyāptayo khilāḥ  MAnuv vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ samākhyā ca tathāvidhāḥ kurupāṇḍavavat teṣāmupapatteḥ pṛthag vacaḥ  MAnuv svanyāyaiḥ sādhanaṃ kāryaṃ paranyāyaistu dūṣaṇam svanyāyairdūṣaṇaṃ ca syāt sādhitaiḥ prativādinaḥ  MAnuv prasaṅgārthatayā proktā na siddhāntasya dūṣakāḥ chalaṃ jātiriti dvedhā vyāhatyantaramiṣyate jātiḥ svavyāhatirjñeyā chalamarthāntarottaram  MAnuv evaṃ saṃśodhitanyāyasadāgamavirodhataḥ nānirvācyamiha proktaṃ māyāmātrapadena hi  MAnuv vilakṣaṇaṃ sadasatoriti hi vyāhataṃ svataḥ pratiyogitvamapyasya brahmaṇo ṅgīkṛtaṃ bhavet  MAnuv mithyā cet pratiyogitvaṃ vailakṣaṇyaṃ tato na hi avilakṣaṇatvaṃ satyaṃ syānmithyātvaṃ brahmaṇastataḥ  MAnuv anirvācyasya sattvaṃ vā yadi dharmā na kecana brahmaṇo naiva jijñāsyaṃ jijñāsā dharmanirṇayaḥ  MAnuv idamitthamiti jñānaṃ jijñāsāyāḥ prayojanam itthambhāvo hi dharmo sya na cenna pratiyogitā  MAnuv itthambhāvātmakān dharmānāhuśca śrutayo khilāḥ adṛśyatvādayo pyasya guṇā hi prabhuṇoditāḥ  MAnuv yadi syustādṛśā dharmāḥ sarvajñatvādayo na kim anyāpekṣā yadi syuṣṭe sattaivaṃ deśakālagā  MAnuv deśakālānapekṣā hi na sattā kvāpi dṛśyate sarvadharmojjñitasyāsya kiṃ śāstreṇādhigamyate  MAnuv mithyādharmavidhātuśca vedasyaivāpramāṇatā aprāptāṃ bhrāntimāpādya kiṃ vedo mānatāṃ vrajet  MAnuv na hi vedaṃ vinā brahma vedyaṃ dharmāśca tadgatāḥ vedavedyasya mithyātvaṃ yadi naikyasya tat katham  MAnuv dharmāropo pi sāmānyadharmādīnāṃ hi daśarne idantadādidharmitve dharmo nyaḥ kalpyate tra hi  MAnuv sarvadharmavihīnasya dharmāropaḥ kva dṛśyate tadarthaṃ yadi dharmāṇāmāropaḥ sānavasthitiḥ  MAnuv īśatajjñānavedākṣajānumāmātṛpūrviṇaḥ bhrāntirviśvasya yenaiva mānābhāsena kalpyate tra hi  MAnuv tanmātrasyānyathā bhāvāt kiṃ na syād viśvasatyatā yenedaṃ kalpyate bhrāntaṃ bhrāntistasyaiva kiṃ na sā  MAnuv bhrāntatve tasya viśvāderīśādyabhrāntameva hi bhaveyurbhrāntayo nṛṇāṃ naiveśādeḥ kathañcana  MAnuv satyatvamakṣajaprāptaṃ yadi bhrāntamitīṣyate prāmāṇyamāgamasyāpi pratyakṣādanyataḥ kutaḥ  MAnuv sākṣipratyakṣato hyeva mānānāṃ mānateyate sākṣiṇaḥ svaprakāśatvamanavasthā tato na hi  MAnuv tātkālikaṃ pramāṇatvamakṣajasya yadā bhavet aikyāgamasya kiṃ na syāt tasyāpyetādṛśaṃ yadi aikyaprāmāṇyamithyātvaṃ yadā viśvasya satyatā  MAnuv aikyāgamasya mānatvaṃ yadyabādhyamitīṣyate akṣajasyāpi mānatvaṃ nābādhyaṃ kimitīṣyate  MAnuv advaitahānisāmānyānna viśeṣaśca kaścana yadi svatastvaṃ prāmāṇye viśvasattā kathaṃ na te  MAnuv prāmāṇyasya ca maryādā kālato vyāhatā bhavet kālāntare pyamānaṃ cedidānīṃ mānatā kutaḥ  MAnuv mithyātvamānaṃ mokṣe pi mānaṃ kiṃ neti bhaṇyatām mānatve dvaitahāniḥ syādamānatve pyamokṣatā  MAnuv viśvasya punarāpattirmithyāmānaṃ yadā na mā asti cenmuktayavasthā ca dvaitāpattirato nyathā  MAnuv amuktatvaṃ tathā kāle kālādhīnā hi muktatā kāla evāgamo pyāha muktiṃ kālanivartane mukterapi nivṛttiḥ syāt saṃsāritvamato bhavet  MAnuv kva ca pratyakṣataḥ prāptamanumāgamabādhitam dehātmatvaṃ yadi na tat prāptaṃ pratyakṣataḥ kvacit mama deha iti hyeva na deho hamiti pramā  MAnuv upacāraśca kṛṣṇo hamiti kardamalepane vastrasya yadvadevaṃ syād yadyupādhikṛtaṃ tadā svataḥ śuklatvavat kārṣṇyaṃ na mameti pratīyate  MAnuv kathaṃ ca bhedo dehāderātmano na pramīyate jātamātrā mṛgā gāvo hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo khaṣāḥ bhayābhayasvabhogādau kāraṇāni vijānate  MAnuv asmṛtau pūrvadehasya vijñānaṃ tat kathaṃ bhavet anvayavyatirekāderanusandhānavismṛtau  MAnuv yadā dehāntarajñānaṃ dehaikyāvasitiḥ kutaḥ vyāptatvādātmano dehe vyavahāreṣvapāṭavāt  MAnuv bhedajñāne pi cāṅgāravahnivat svāviviktavat bhavanti vyavahārāśca na hi pratyakṣagānapi  MAnuv arthān yathānubhavataḥ pratipādayituṃ kṣamāḥ lokāstato hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ nānyena kenacit  MAnuv śakyaṃ vārayituṃ kvāpi taccennottaragocaram kathamevottaraḥ kālastadgo mokṣaśca gamyate  MAnuv āgamo pi hi sāmānye siddhe pratyakṣataḥ punaḥ viśeṣaṃ gamayedeva kathaṃ śaktigraho nyathā  MAnuv atītānāgatārtheṣu jāte śaktigrahe khilam viśeṣaṃ jñāpayed vākyaṃ na tadajñātaśaktike  MAnuv śaktiśced vartamāne syānnātītānāgataṃ vadet yadi śaktigraho nyatra kathaṃ sa syāt tadagrahe  MAnuv sāmānyaṃ dṛṣṭamevāsāvanyatra gamayed yadi sāmānyavarjitaṃ vastusvarūpaṃ gamayet katham  MAnuv na svarūpatvasāmānyaṃ kenāpyaṅgīkṛtaṃ kvacit svarūpaṃ cedanugataṃ vyāvṛttaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet  MAnuv sarvānugatadharmāṇāmante hi svatvamiṣyate kiṃ vyāvṛttamiti praśne svarūpamiti kevalam syāduttaraṃ tato nyaccet tadeva svayameva naḥ  MAnuv evaṃ vyāvṛttarūpe pi yadā śaktigraho bhavet tasya sāmānyato jñānaṃ vinā sa ca bhavet kutaḥ  MAnuv ato viśeṣasāmānyarūpaṃ sarvamapīṣyate vyāvṛttaṃ yacca sāmānyaṃ tadeva syād viśeṣataḥ  MAnuv nacaikadharmatā tena padārthānāṃ parasparam dharmāṇāṃ bhedadṛṣṭayaiva tatsādṛśyasya darśanāt  MAnuv ataḥ sarvapadārthāśca sāmānyāt sākṣigocarāḥ sarvamityeva vijñānaṃ sarveṣāṃ kathamanyathā  MAnuv kiñcitsādṛśyavijñānādakhilasyāpi vastunaḥ śabdaśaktigrahaśca syāt tattatsādṛśyamānataḥ  MAnuv pratyakṣaṃ mānasaṃ caiva yadātītārthagocaram tadā smṛtipramāṇatvamatītatvaviśeṣitam  MAnuv ādhikyamanubhūtāttu yadātītatvamiṣyate mānatā ca kathaṃ na syāt smṛterbādhaśca nātrahi  MAnuv mānatvaṃ pratyabhijñāyā api sarvānubhūtigam atītavartamānatvadharmiṇī sā ca dṛśyate  MAnuv na ca sā smṛtimātrārdhā tadidantvagrahaikataḥ ato na vatarmānaikaniyamaḥ syād grahe kṣaje  MAnuv na ca pramāṇato nyā syāt pramitirnāma kutracit mānābhāvād gauravācca kalpanāyāḥ kimetayā  MAnuv mayaitajjñātamiti tu sākṣigaṃ jñānagocaram jñānameva tato nyā na pramitirnāma dṛśyate  MAnuv mānāmātṛprameyāṇāṃ taducchittirnahi kvacit svapnānāmapi caiteṣāṃ na bādho dṛśyate kvacit  MAnuv jāgrattvamātramatraikamanyathā dṛśyate sphuṭam ato mithyā na ca svapno jāgradvajjāgradeva ca  MAnuv ātmavat kvacidātmā ca syādeva bhramagocaraḥ etāvatā na mithyāsau svapne jāgarite tathā  MAnuv yadyātmanyanyathā dṛśyaṃ bhrāntamatrāpi tad bhavet abādhitānuvṛttestu svapnāderbhrāntatā kutaḥ  MAnuv na ca kācit pramā viśvabhrāntatve sarvameva ca abhrāntatve pramāṇaṃ tu kathaṃ tadbhrāntitā bhavet  MAnuv kiñca bhrāntatvavādī sa bhrāntatvaṃ svamatasya ca aṅgīkaroti niyataṃ tatra sampratipannatā vādinostena cābhrāntaṃ viśvameva bhaviṣyati  MAnuv bhrāntitvabhrāntatā cet syāt kathaṃ nābhrāntisatyatā aśeṣadoṣaduṣyaṃ tanmataṃ heyaṃ bubhūṣibhiḥ  MAnuv yena svamataheyatvaṃ svayamaṅgīkṛtaṃ sadā bhrāntitvād durghaṭatvasya bhūṣaṇatvācca kevalam  MAnuv unmatto pi kathaṃ tasya mataṃ svīkartumicchati īśaśakteracintyatvānmahonmattaiḥ pravartitam  MAnuv ataḥ prajñātra māyoktā jaivyupādānameva sā nimittamaiśvarī mukhyaṃ nirmitaṃ trātameva ca  MAnuv tābhyāṃ saha pṛthak caiva māyāmātramitīryate ubhābhyāṃ mātamaiśvaryā trātaṃ saha pṛthak tataḥ  MAnuv prajñātmakaṃ mano yena manorūpāśca vāsanāḥ dhīrbhīriti manastvevetyāha ca śrutirañjasā  MAnuv cidacinmiśramevaitanmano yāvacca saṃsṛtiḥ tenāvasthā imāḥ sarvā jīvaḥ paśyati sarvadā  MAnuv manovikārā viṣayāḥ svāpnā yad bahyavanna te sthūlā bhavantyatasteṣāṃ spaṣṭatā na tathā kvacit  MAnuv kvacit spaṣṭā api syuṣye vāsanā mānasī ca sā īśecchayāntardadhāti vyajyate ca punastayā  MAnuv sṛṣṭvaiva vāsānabhiśca prapañcaṃ svāpnamīśvaraḥ vāsanāmātratāṃ tasya nītvāntardhāpayatyajaḥ  MAnuv suṣuptimohabodhāṃśca svavaśastadvaśaṃ sadā jīvaṃ nayati deveśo nānyaḥ kartāsya kaścana  MAnuv na sthānabhedato pyasya bhedaḥ kaścit pareśituḥ sarvatrāśeṣadoṣojkhapūrṇakalyāṇacidguṇaḥ  MAnuv tadviruddhaṃ tu yat tatra mānaṃ naiva bhavet kvacit mahātātparyarodhena kathaṃ tanmānamatra tu  MAnuv duḥkhāpyayasukhāvāptihetutvenaiva vedavāk bhavenmānaṃ tadīśānāt prasannādeva nānyathā  MAnuv prasannatā guṇotkarṣajñānādeva hi kevalam nirdoṣatāparijñānādapi nānyena kenacit  MAnuv yo māmaśeṣadoṣojkhaṃ guṇasarvasvabṛṃhitam jānātyasmai prasanno haṃ dadyāṃ muktiṃ nacānyathā  MAnuv yo māmaśeṣābhyadhikaṃ vijānāti sa eva mām vijānātyakhilāṃstasya dadyāṃ kāmān paraṃ padam  MAnuv yo māmevamasammūḍhaḥ kiṃ mā nindanti śatravaḥ ityādivedasmṛtigavākyairevāvasīyate  MAnuv lokataśca prasādena muktiḥ sa guṇavedanāt mahātātparyamukhyasya virodhādata eva hi  MAnuv doṣitvanirguṇatvālpaguṇatvādi kathañcana nārthaḥ śrutipurāṇādestadviruddho khilasya ca arthaḥ svayaṃ vinirṇīto vāsudevena sādaram  MAnuv iti guhyatamaṃ śāstramidamuktaṃ mayānagha etad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaśca bhārata  MAnuv ityato khilasacchāstraviruddhatvena nānumā vartate tatra teneśo nirṇīto khilasadguṇaḥ  MAnuv na ca cittvādabhinnatvaṃ jīvasyeśavadāpyate yata ābhāsatāmeva śrutirasya vadatyalam  MAnuv yathaiṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasminnetadātatam chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśā pumādhīnā ca dṛśyate evamevātmakāḥ sarve brahmādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ  MAnuv sattāpratītikāryeṣu pumadhīno yatheyate ābhāsa eva puruṣā muktāśca paramātmanaḥ  MAnuv chāyā viṣṇo ramā tasyāśchāyā dhātā viśeṣakau tasyendrakāmau ca tayostayoranye khilā api  MAnuv harerbrahmāsya gīstasyā viśeṣāvindra etayoḥ māraścābhāsakāḥ sarva etayostadadhīnataḥ  MAnuv sarve lpaśaktayaścaiva pūrṇaśaktiḥ paro hariḥ cetanatve pi bhinnāste tasmādetena sarvadā ityādiśrutivākyebhyo jñāyate bheda eva hi  MAnuv ābhāsatvaṃ hi nirṇītaṃ jīvasya paramātmanaḥ tanna yuktaṃ yadābhāsa upādhyāyatta īyate  MAnuv upādhyāyattatābhāvādābhāsatvavirodhataḥ cetanatvena cāṃśatvāt samudāyaikyamāpatet  MAnuv ataḥ pṛthaktavamuditaṃ samudāyāṃśayorbhavet īśākhyā samudāye syādīśarūpeṣvivoditā  MAnuv ato dehādyupādhīnāmapāye samatā bhavet īśarūpairathābhāsā mukhyataḥ sūryakādivat  MAnuv yadā tadopādhyāyattarūpāṇāṃ nāśitā bhavet ityāśaṅkānivṛttyarthamāha vedādhipaḥ prabhuḥ ata evopametyeva cānyābhāsaviśeṣitām  MAnuv yaduktaṃ tadadhīnatvaṃ sarvāvasthāsvaśeṣataḥ jīvasya sadṛśatvaṃ ca cittvamātraṃ nacāparam  MAnuv tāvanmātreṇa cābhāso rūpameṣāṃ cidātmanām nopādhyadhīnatādyaiśca nātisāmyaṃ nidarśane  MAnuv kiñcitsukhādisādṛśyamapīśenesurānṛte tata ābhāsate nityaṃ tadvadābhāsate pi ca  MAnuv bhānamastitvamapicaivāsamantād yatastataḥ jīva ābhāsa uddiṣṭaḥ sadaiva paramātmanaḥ  MAnuv na jalāyattasūryādipratibimbopamatvataḥ tadadhīnatvameveti kiñcit sādṛśyameva ca samprakāśayataḥ sūtragatāvakhilamānataḥ  MAnuv jīveśabhedadṛṣṭayaiva samudāyaikatā kutaḥ aśeṣadoṣarāhityaṃ sarvaśaktitvato hareḥ  MAnuv sarvopeteti kathitamata aikyaṃ kva doṣiṇā aśeṣaśaktiyuktaścet svātantryād doṣavān katham  MAnuv anusandhānarahitamaikyaṃ cedekatā na tat cetanaikye nusandhānaṃ pramāṇaṃ naiva cāparam  MAnuv anusandhānarahitasamudāyaikyameva cet cetaneṣvastu tannāmamātrameva yatastataḥ  MAnuv muktau syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet sarvajña ekatāṃ nānusandhatte naiva sā yataḥ  MAnuv paścāt syādanusandhānaṃ cenmithyājñānitā bhavet vidyamānānusandhānaṃ na cedajñatvamāpatet  MAnuv asadaikyaṃ bhavet paścād yadi syāt saptamo rasaḥ samudāyaikyametasmād dūrato pākṛtaṃ sadā  MAnuv ato śeṣaguṇonnaddhaṃ nirdoṣaṃ yāvadeva hi tāvadeveśvaro nāma tatra bhedo pi na kvacit  MAnuv neha nānāsti kimapi harayo yamayaṃ hi saḥ ityādiśrutimānena jīvāṃśāḥ sarva eva ca  MAnuv niyamenānusandhānavanto yadyekatā svataḥ aṃśino śeṣasandhānamatyalpasyāpi vidyate  MAnuv bhuvi jātena cāṃśena sukhaduḥkhādi tadgatam anubhūyate viśeṣastu kaścidīśakṛto bhavet  MAnuv īśasyācintyaśaktitvānnāśakyaṃ kvāpi vidyate seśatānupapannaiva yadi jīvaikatāsya hi anīśasyeśatetyeva viruddhaṃ sarvamānataḥ  MAnuv īśatvenaiva vijñātamanīśatvena cecchrutiḥ anīśatvena vijñātamīśatvenāthavā diśet  MAnuv upajīvyavirodhena naiva mānatvameṣyati ata eveśatāsiddherna kiñcicchakyamasya ca  MAnuv īśatve nīśabhedena śrutyā samyak prakāśite ayuktamapi cānyatra yuktaṃ bhavati tadbalāt  MAnuv ato nyatrāpi yad dṛṣṭaṃ tadīśenaiva kalpyate śrutyābhāsāptamapi nahīśatvaparipanthi yat  MAnuv īśo nīśo jaganmithyā duḥkhī mukto bhidā na hi iti pratijñāvyāghātaḥ sarvadoṣādhikādhikaḥ  MAnuv iti hi brahmatarkoktiratiheyamato khilaiḥ bubhūṣubhirmatamidaṃ jīveśābhedavādinaḥ  MAnuv nāyuktamīśituḥ kiñcidīśatvasyāvirodhi yat yadīśitvavirodhi syāt tadevāyuktamañjasā  MAnuv īśitvasyāvirodhena yojayitvākhilāḥ pramāḥ siddheśitvena cāyuktamapi hīśe na yojayet  MAnuv mānataḥ prāptamakhilaṃ nāmānaṃ yojayet kvacit iti hi brahmatarkoktirato yuktamihoditam  MAnuv sa cāprākṛtarūpatvādarūpaḥ svaguṇaśatmakam rūpamasya śiraḥpāṇipādādyātmakamiṣyate  MAnuv ato nānityatā naiva śrutidvayavirodhitā yathā hi taijasasyaiva prakāśasyojkhitāvapi ātmaiva jyotirityāha jīvasyeśaṃ śrutistathā  MAnuv tadbhaktitāratamyena tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam brahmādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāmānandāderyathākramam  MAnuv pratibimbavadapyeṣāmānando nyaguṇā yathā nārāyaṇaguṇādhīnaścātyalpastadapekṣayā  MAnuv tasmād bhinnaśca satatamanyajjñānaṃ parasya ca anyajjñānaṃ tu jīvānāmanya ānanda īśatā  MAnuv mukhyeśatā pareśasya gauṇī jīvasya sā yataḥ iti śruteḥ sṛṣṭināśau tadadhīnāvitīrite svabhāvatvāt sthiternaitadapekṣeti na yujyate  MAnuv yataḥ svabhāvo khila īśāyatto khilasya ca avyakto pi svaktayaiva bhaktānāṃ dṛśyate hariḥ  MAnuv tadabhinnā guṇā nityamapi sarve viśeṣataḥ guṇatvena guṇitvena bhoktṛbhogyatayā sthitāḥ  MAnuv viśeṣātmatayā teṣāṃ nityaśaktayātmanā tathā nityasthiterna dharmāṇāṃ kriyādīnāmanityatā  MAnuv na viśeṣātmatā ceyamanityā śaktirūpatā saiva yat saviśeṣā syād viśeṣo nyo nacāpyayam  MAnuv svanirvāhakatāhetostathāpi syād viśeṣataḥ viśeṣatvena vijñāteḥ pramāṇairakhilairapi  MAnuv sasarja sañjahāreti viśeṣo hyavagamyate śrutyaiva sa sa eveti tadabhedaśca gamyate  MAnuv bhedo yadi viśeṣasya sa bhedo bhedinā katham bhinnaścedanavasthā syādabhinnaścet purā na kim  MAnuv viśeṣo bhinna eveti tena nābhyupagamyate abhinno nivirśeṣaśced bhedastadbhedatā kutaḥ  MAnuv anenānena bhinno yamiti yat sa viśeṣataḥ bheda evaiṣa bahudhā dṛśyate tat kimuttaram  MAnuv abhedabhedayoścaiva svarūpatvaṃ hi bhedinā tayorapyaviśeṣatve paryāyatvaṃ hi śabdayoḥ  MAnuv abhedabhedaśabdau ca paryāyāviti ko vadet bhedo nyonyamabhedaśca bhedinā ced viśeṣatā  MAnuv nirviśeṣe kathaṃ bhedo bhedinaikastathābhidā punastayorvibhedaśca kalpyate tadā  MAnuv aikyapratītyabhāvena bheda eva gavaśvayoḥ sa eveti pratītau hi viśeṣo nāma bhaṇyate  MAnuv saccidāderaparyāyasiddhayarthaṃ māyināpi hi aṅgīkāryo viśeṣo yaṃ yadyasatyaviśeṣaṇam yamevaiṣa iti śrutyā tameveti ca sādaram śāstrayonitvamasyaiva jñāyate vedavādibhiḥ  MAnuv ya enaṃ viduramṛtā ityuktastu samudragaḥ tadeva brahma paramamiti śrutyāvadhāritaḥ  MAnuv yataḥ prasūteti pratyakṣāgamamūlakāḥ  MAnuv pratyakṣamaiśvaraṃ caiva ramādīnāmaśeṣataḥ muktānāmapyamuktānāmetamevārthamuttamam  MAnuv anyāvakāśarahitaṃ prakāśayati sādaram etadeva ca sacchāstraṃ duḥśāstraṃ tu tataḥ param  MAnuv sacchāstramabhyasennityaṃ duḥśāstraṃ ca parityajet asaṃśayena tattvasya nirṇaye brahmadarśanam  MAnuv samyagviṣamavijñānatāratamyānusārataḥ phalaṃ bhavet tāratamyāt sukhaduḥkhātmakaṃ nṛṇām  MAnuv samyak cādhikavijñānāt sukhādhikyaṃ bhavennṛṇām ato yathātmaśaktayaiva śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ tathā  MAnuv viṣayeṣu ca saṃsargācchāśvatasya ca saṃśayāt manasā cānyadākāṅkṣāt paraṃ na pratipādyate  MAnuv iti bhāratavākyaṃ hi tenaitaddoṣavarjitaḥ sadopāsanayā yukto vāsudevaṃ prapaśyati  MAnuv doṣā anādisambaddhāste muktiparipanthinaḥ santyeva prāyaśaḥ puṃsu tena mokṣo na jāyate  MAnuv sarve ta ete jīveṣu dṛśyante tāratamyataḥ ṛjūnāmeka evāsti paramotsāhavarjanam sa guṇālpatvamātratvānnarjatvena viruddhayate  MAnuv ato viṣṇau parā bhaktistadbhakteṣu ramādiṣu tāratamyena kartavyā puruṣārthamabhīpsitā  MAnuv svādaraḥ sarvajantūnāṃ saṃsiddho hi svabhāvataḥ tato dhikaḥ svottameṣu tadādhikyānusārataḥ  MAnuv kartavyo vāsudevāntaṃ sarvathā śubhamicchatā na kadācit tyajet taṃ ca krameṇainaṃ vivardhayet  MAnuv sameṣu svātmavat snehaḥ satsvanyatra tato dayā kāryaivamāparokṣyeṇa dṛśyate kṣipramīśvaraḥ  MAnuv tat tamo ndhaṃ vrajed viṣṇusamatvaṃ yo nupaśyati ramābrahmaśivādīnāmapi muktau kathañcana  MAnuv kimutādhikyadṛṣṭestad guṇābhāvamaterapi doṣavetturabhedasya draṣṭurdraṣṭustathobhayoḥ  MAnuv ityāha sacchrutistena samproktaguṇasaṃyutam upāsīta hariṃ dṛṣṭvā muktistenaiva jāyate  MAnuv dveṣād yanmuktikathanaṃ śrutivākyavirodhi yat ripavo ye tu rāmasya vimukhatvānnirāmiṇaḥ abhidrohapade nityamandhe tamasi te sthitāḥ  MAnuv haridviṣastamo yānti ye caiva tadabhedinaḥ tannirguṇatvavettārastasya doṣavido pi ca  MAnuv ityādiśrutisandarbhād dveṣiṇastama īyate hiraṇyakaśipuścāpi bhagavannindayā tamaḥ vidhikṣuratyagāt sūno prahlādasyānubhāvataḥ  MAnuv yadanindat pitā mahyaṃ tvadbhakte mayi cāghavān tasmāt pitā me pūyeta durantād dustarādaghāt  MAnuv nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃstatparasya janasya vā tato nāpaiti yaḥ so pi yātyaghaḥ sukṛtāccyutaḥ  MAnuv avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram  MAnuv moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ  MAnuv māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto bhyasūyakāḥ tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu  MAnuv āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim  MAnuv yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum kathaṃ sa na bhaved dveṣya ālokāntasya kasyacit  MAnuv yo dviṣṭād vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum majjanti pitarastasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ityādivākyasandohād dveṣiṇastama eva tu  MAnuv naiva mokṣa iti prāhurlokāyatamate sthitāḥ bhogaḥ śarīraparyantaṃ bhasmībhāvastato bhavet  MAnuv iti tat kena mānena dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣavādinā na hi pratyakṣamānena mokṣābhāvo vasīyate  MAnuv ghaṭate muktidṛṣṭistu puruṣeṇa mahīyasā neti vakturmahattvaṃ tu kathañcana na vidyate  MAnuv sādhayan sarvasāmānyaṃ kathameva viśeṣavān dṛśyante puruṣā loke parāvaravido pica  MAnuv aparokṣadṛśo yoganiṣṭhāścāmalacakṣuṣaḥ pratyakṣaṃ devatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatprasādāptabhūtayaḥ  MAnuv jñānavijñānapārajñā niṣiddhayante kathaṃ nṛbhiḥ dṛśyate cātimāhātmyaṃ teṣāmatimahaujasām  MAnuv yadi te pi niṣiddhayante kiṃ noktiste niṣiddhayate yaduktavākyaprāmāṇyaṃ pratyakṣeṇopalabhyate  MAnuv varādayo pi taddattāḥ sadā satyā bhavanti hi aprāmāṇyaṃ tadukteśca vṛthāvācāvasīyate  MAnuv na hi prayojanaṃ kiñcit paralokanivāraṇāt vṛthāvācaṃ vṛthā hanyād yadi tasya kimuttaram svajīvanavirodhāya vadan kiṃ nāma buddhimān  MAnuv prāmāṇye saṃśayaḥ kiṃ syāt tayoḥ puruṣayorapi svajīvanaviruddhoktirajño dṛṣṭasya cāpi saḥ  MAnuv yaścātīndriyadevoktiśrotā dṛṣṭaparāvaraḥ atītānāgataṃ sarvaṃ lokānubhavamāpayan ataḥ pratyakṣagamyatvād vedamātvasya ca sphuṭam  MAnuv yadyāgamasya no mātvamakṣajasya tathā bhavet yadyakṣajasya mātvaṃ syādāgamasya kathaṃ na tat lokavākyād viśeṣaścāvyabhicāreṇa siddhayati  MAnuv asti mokṣo pi dharmeṇa yathārthajñānato pi ca prāmāṇyamanumāyāśca jinasyāptatvasādhane  MAnuv tadvākyād dharmasajjñānavijñaptirbhavatīti ca dharmo hiṃsāparo nānyo jñānaṃ pudgaladarśanam  MAnuv iti jaināḥ kathaṃ tat syāt pramāṇamanumānataḥ viṣayān prati sthitaṃ hyakṣaṃ pratyakṣamiti gīyate pratyakṣaśabdānusārādanumeti prakītirtā  MAnuv ā samantād gamayati dharmādharmau paraṃ padam yaccāpyatīndriyaṃ tvanyat tenāsāvāgamaḥ smṛtaḥ  MAnuv etena kāreṇenaiva tattanmānatvamiṣyate svarūpaṃ hi tadeteṣāmanyathāsiddhimānataḥ  MAnuv ato numā kathaṃ dharmaṃ pudgalaṃ cāpi darśayet svarūpaṃ pudgalasyoktā doṣā ānandameva ca na manyate pudgalaṃ sa duḥkhābhāvaḥ sukhaṃ tviti  MAnuv mātrābhogātirekeṇa sukhādhikyasya darśanāt sukhasyābhāvatā kena na ca syāt kiṃ viparyayaḥ  MAnuv yadi bhāvo pi kaścit syāt tasyaivābhāvatā kutaḥ yadi sarve pyabhāvāḥ syuranyonyamiti bhāvatā  MAnuv abhāvābhāvatā yat syāt kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tadā bhavet bhāvatvaṃ vidhirūpatvaṃ niṣedhatvamabhāvatā  MAnuv niṣedhasya niṣedho pi bhāva eva balād bhavet prathamapratipattistu bhāvabhāvaniyāmikā  MAnuv na ca pudgalavijñānaṃ mokṣadaṃ bhavati kvacit asvātantryāt pudgalasya jñāto pi sukhado na hi  MAnuv na hi duḥkhiparijñānād duḥkhitvaṃ vinivartate yadi pudgalavijñānādaduḥkhī syāt kathañcana dehavānapi nāduḥkhī kiṃ jñānāduttaraṃ sadā  MAnuv īśakḷptyanusāreṇa syāt kālādīśavādinaḥ karmahetutvamapi tu niścaitanyānnahi kvacit  MAnuv aśeṣaduḥkhavilaye nedānīṃ kāraṇaṃ yathā tathottaraṃ ca naiva syād dṛṣṭipūrvānumā yataḥ  MAnuv śaktasyānyasya vijñānaṃ tatprītijanakaṃ yadi tayaiva bandhahāniḥ syāditi kiṃ nāma dūṣaṇam  MAnuv svajñānād bandhahānistu dṛśyate kasya kutracit ahiṃsāyāśca dharmatvaṃ kena mānena gamyate hiṃsāyā eva dharmatvamityukte syāt kimuttaram  MAnuv dharmasya sukhahetutvamapi kenāvagamyate hatyayā mokṣahetutvaṃ kuto mānānnivāryate  MAnuv na ca śūnyaparijñānācchūnyabhāvanayāpi ca mokṣaḥ kathañcana bhaved yadīdānīṃ kathaṃ na saḥ  MAnuv paraprasādanecchostu viḷambo nāma yujyate pumicchādhīnatā no ced viḷambaḥ kiṅkṛto bhavet  MAnuv anyatrāpi viḷambāstu syurīśecchānimittataḥ anyathā kāraṇaṃ cet syāt kiṃ kāryaṃ nopajāyate kāraṇe sati kāryasya bhāvaḥ suniyato sya hi  MAnuv vijñānavādinaścaiva vijñānādvaitavedanāt vijñānabhāvanāccaiva mokṣo na ghaṭate kvacit  MAnuv antarjñānasya bāhye ca kṣaṇikatvasya vedanāt bhāvanāccoktamārgeṇa mānābhāvānna mucyate  MAnuv prakṛteḥ puruṣasyāpi viveko muktisādhanam iti śaṅkayā na caitasmin mānamīśāprasādataḥ  MAnuv śrutayaḥ smṛtayaścaiva yadīśasya prasādataḥ vadanti niyamānmuktiṃ tamṛte taḥ kuto bhavet  MAnuv kaṇādayogākṣapādā apīśasya prasādataḥ muktiṃ bruvāṇā apyāhurbhogādeva ca karmaṇām kṣayaṃ prāhuḥ kutaścaitat prasanne jagadīśvare  MAnuv bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare  MAnuv bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi dṛṣṭa evātmanīśvare iti śrutipurāṇādivacanebhyo nyathāgateḥ  MAnuv na ca pāśupatādyuktaśivādīnāmanugrahāt nānyaḥ panthā iti hyuktaṃ puruṣajñānataḥ śrutau  MAnuv sarve nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣādataḥ evaṃ puruṣaśabdaśca prayukto bdhiśaye harau  MAnuv na tasyeśe kaścana tasya nāma mahad yaśaḥ iti cādhipatistasya pratiṣiddhaḥ svayaṃ śrutau  MAnuv viśvataḥ paramāṃ nityaṃ viśvaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim iti sarvādhikatvoktayā samo pi vinivāritaḥ samādhikasya rāhityānnopacārapumānasau  MAnuv puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyam utāmṛtatvasyeśāno yadannenātirohati  MAnuv muktāmuktapareśatvamiti tasyāha sā śrutiḥ amṛteśānavacanāt sarvasyeśānatoditā  MAnuv yadi sarvatvamuditamuteśa iti tad vṛthā utaśabdo vadedeṣa hīśatvasya samuccayam  MAnuv puruṣeṇedaṃ vyāptamiti brāhmaṇaṃ cāha taṃ prati etāvānasya mahimeti mahimno vaco hi tat  MAnuv so mṛtasyābhayasyeśo martyamannaṃ yadatyagāt ityamuktādhipatyaṃ tu pūrvārdhoktamanūdya ca  MAnuv utāmṛtasyeśa iti vidhatte muktigeśatām ato viṣṇuparijñānādeva muktirnacānyataḥ tad yatheti śruteścaiva tataḥ karmakṣayo bhavet  MAnuv yathaidhāṃsi samiddho gnirbhasmasāt kurute rjuna jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā  MAnuv sarvadharmān parityajya māmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ ityādibhagavadvākyairuktārthaścāvasīyate  MAnuv nityanaimittikaṃ karma kurvannanyat parityajan mucyate saṃsṛteścaitadapyetena nirākṛtam vidyaivetīmamevārthaṃ svayamevāha vedarāṭ  MAnuv vinā karma na mokṣaḥ syājjñānenetyapi sā śrutiḥ nānyaḥ panthā iti hyeva nivārayati sādaram  MAnuv anyathopāsanamapi tamevamitivādinī nivārayatyādareṇa na pratīka iti prabhuḥ  MAnuv andhaṃ tamaḥ praviśanti ye vidyāmupāsate iti śrutivirodhācca nānyathopāsanaṃ bhavet  MAnuv na cāpyekatvavijñānāduktanyāyena mucyate iti sarvaṃ pravijñāya sarvaistarkasadāgamaiḥ upāsīta hariṃ nityaṃ guṇaireva svayogataḥ  MAnuv brahmā sarvaiguṇaiścaiva kriyāsāmānyataśca gīḥ guṇasāmānyato rudro dravyasāmānyataḥ pare  MAnuv adhikāraviśeṣeṇa bhaktijñānasukhādibhiḥ viśeṣo devatādīnāṃ mokṣe caiva viśeṣataḥ  MAnuv na tāvatā virodho sti nirdoṣatvāt samastaśaḥ ābhāsatvāt pareṣāṃ tadavarāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ  MAnuv yato varāṇāṃ sarve pi guṇāḥ sarvāḥ kriyā api niyamenaiva pūrveṣāṃ suprasādanibandhanāḥ ataḥ sacchiṣyavat teṣāṃ naiverṣyādiḥ kathañcana  MAnuv na ca saṃsāridevānāṃ kāleyattāpare ime sūtre hyārabdhamātrasya bhogenaiva kṣayo dhruvaḥ  MAnuv anārabdhakārye bhogena tvitare iti coditaḥ paunaruktayena tenaite uktārthe iti niścayaḥ  MAnuv uṣāḥ svāhā ca parjanyo mitro gnirvaruṇo vidhuḥ pravaho niruddha indrome rudro vāṇī ca mārutaḥ uttarottaratastvete guṇaiḥ sarvaiśca muktigāḥ  MAnuv sūryadharmau yathā somo manurdakṣo bṛhaspatiḥ śacī ratiścāniruddhasamāstārā ca mitravat  MAnuv somavacchatarūpā tu prasūtirvahnivad virāṭ parjanyavad vāruṇī ca tathā sañjñā ca rohiṇī  MAnuv dharmī ca mitravattvena prāvahī parikīrtitā mitrapajarnyamadhyasthāvaśvinau vighnavittapau  MAnuv bhṛguragnisamo mitratanmadhye brahmaputrakāḥ varuṇāgnyantarā tatra nāradaḥ prāya indravat  MAnuv kāmaḥ suparṇī comāvad vīndro rudravadīritaḥ niṛtirmitrasadṛśo viśvāmitraḥ kasūnuvat  MAnuv vaivasvato manuścāśvipaścādanye tato varāḥ cyavanocathyavainyāśca śaśabinduśca haihayaḥ tadvacca viprarājanyaviśeṣo trāpi kaścana  MAnuv tadvat priyavrataścāpi tadanyāḥ śatadevatāḥ pajarnyamitrāntarāḷe tadanye tu tato varāḥ  MAnuv etebhyo bhyadhikā śrīrastu sadā muktā viśeṣataḥ tatsamo nāsti paramo harireva nacāparaḥ  MAnuv saṃhitāyāṃ bṛhatyāṃ tu svayaṃ bhagavatoditam tadetadakhilaṃ prāṇa āhaṅkārika eva ca indrādanantaro dṛṣṭirapi yogyānusārataḥ  MAnuv samyag guruprasādaśca mukhyato dṛṣṭikāraṇam śravaṇādi ca kartavyaṃ nānyathā darśanaṃ kvacit  MAnuv guṇādhikaṃ guruṃ prāpya taddhīnaṃ nāpnuyāt kvacit viparyayastu kartavyaḥ sarvathā muktimicchatā  MAnuv same vikalpa eva syāt pūrvānujñā ca sarvathā taduttamaguruprāptyai pūrvānujñā na mṛgyate  MAnuv gurubarrahmākhilānāṃ ca vidyā caiva sarasvatī devatā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ  MAnuv tatprasādena muktiḥ syānnānyathā tu kathañcana svottamāstu krameṇaiva sarveṣāṃ guravaḥ śrutāḥ upadeśo brahmaṇastu sarveṣāmeva muktaye  MAnuv sādhanebhyo dhikā bhaktirnaivānyat tādṛśaṃ kvacit bhaktiścaiva harāveva mukhyānyatra yathākramam  MAnuv svādhikā tveva sarvatra svottameṣu krameṇa ca anuvartate ca sā bhaktirmuktāvānandarūpiṇī tatpūrvakopāsanaivaṃ kartavyā muktaye guṇaiḥ  MAnuv  iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ evamutpannanirdoṣabhagavaddarśanāt sadā apekṣitaphalaprāptirārabdhasyānatikramāt  MAnuv devarṣimānuṣādīnāṃ tattajjātyanusārataḥ jaiminyuktaṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ tadviśeṣāśca kecana  MAnuv sāmānyaṃ bhagavatproktaṃ devādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ balavadvirodhisadbhāve jaiminyādyuktiriṣyate  MAnuv vikarmalepo naivāsti samyagdṛṣṭimatāṃ kvacit guṇahāniśca naivāsti brahmaṇastvavikarmataḥ  MAnuv devānāmapi na prāyaḥ kḷptasya tu kathañcana prāptahrāso bhavet kvāpi mahatā tu vikarmaṇā tathāpi tat kḷptameva tasmānna niyamojkhitiḥ  MAnuv candrasugrīvayoścaiva svoccadāraparigrahāt prāptahānirabhūnnaiva kḷptahāniḥ yathañcana  MAnuv hrāso pi mānuṣādīnāmānandasya vikarmaṇā bhavenmuktau viśeṣeṇa svoccānāmaparādhataḥ  MAnuv jñānottarasya pāpasya caturthe lepa ucyate aśucitvādikaṃ tasya na bhavediti tatphalam atra jñānaphalasyaiva mukterniyatatocyate  MAnuv prārabdhakarmajasyaiva viṣabhakṣānmṛteriva prāptasyāpyanivartyasya kiñcid bhuktasya saṃvidā upamarda iha prokto devādīnāṃ yathākramam  MAnuv sarvātmanā tvabhogo hi prārabdhasyaiva karmaṇaḥ na brahmadarśino pi syāt phalahrāsastu vidyate  MAnuv sarvātmanā phalahrāso yadi nārabdhakarmaṇaḥ syāt kāmyavidhivaiyarthyamityuktaniyamo bhavet evamadyāpi samproktaṃ tantrabhāgavate sphuṭam  MAnuv tāratamyaṃ phale no ced brahmādīnāṃ kathaṃ śrutiḥ avṛjino kāmahata iti muktiṃ nigadya ca ānandatāratamyaṃ ca teṣāṃ brūyāt pṛthak pṛthak  MAnuv saṃsāra eva cedetat tāratamyaṃ na mukhyataḥ akāmahataśabdārtho vṛjinatvaṃ ca no bhavet  MAnuv kāmasya yatrāptāḥ kāmāstatra māmamṛtaṃ kṛdhi iti yallakṣaṇaṃ mukteḥ śrutirāha balīyasī  MAnuv kāmāhatiḥ kuto nyatra prāptakāmasya sā bhavet aprayatnena kāmānāmavāptiḥ sā yadā bhavet tadaivākāmahatatā kuta evānyathā bhavet  MAnuv cetanasya tvasuptasya kutra dṛṣṭā hyakāmatā avyaktireva kāmānāṃ na nāśo mohasuptayoḥ  MAnuv yatkāmaḥ svāpamāpnoti tadevotthāpitaḥ kutaḥ avaśo pi vyāharati kutaḥ suptāvakāmatā  MAnuv sarvakāmānavāpnoti brahmaṇā saha muktigaḥ paryeti tatra jakṣaṃśca krīḍan ratimavāpnuvan  MAnuv kāmānnī kāmarūpī sannimān lokāṃśca sañcaran āste gāyan sāma mukta ityādiśrutisadbalāt  MAnuv akāmaḥ syāt kathaṃ muktaḥ kāmā ye sya hṛdi śritāḥ ityantaḥkaraṇasthānāṃ kāmānāṃ mokṣameva hi āha śrutirhṛdītyeva na ced vyarthaṃ viśeṣaṇam  MAnuv hṛdyeṣa teṣāṃ śrayaṇamiti pakṣo na bhāsate muktānāṃ kāmitāmāha pṛthakchākhāsu yacchrutiḥ  MAnuv ato kāmahatatvaṃ tu muktānāmeva mukhyataḥ mukhyārthasya vṛthā tyāgo māyināmeva bhūṣaṇam  MAnuv apāpatvamaduḥkhatvaṃ cāvṛjinatvamihoditam apriyaṃ vṛjinaṃ duḥkhamakaṃ toda itīyarte  MAnuv tatkāraṇatvāt pāpaṃ vā vṛjinaṃ nāma kathyate ityuktaḥ svayamīśena nāmārthaḥ śabdanirṇaye  MAnuv apāpatvaṃ ca naivāsti yāvatsaṃsāramasya hi ārabdhapāpamastyeva duḥkhaṃ ca jñānino pi hi  MAnuv tasmāt tasmādakāmatvamiti cāśrutakalpanā akāmahata ityukteḥ śrutahānirapi sphuṭā  MAnuv kutracit kāminaḥ puṃsaḥ kāmābhāvāt kvacit kvacit indrādisukhabhogo stītyanubhūtirhi kupyati  MAnuv tasmādamuktasukhagaṃ tāratamyaṃ pṛthak pṛthak uktvā yaśceti muktānāṃ tāratamyaṃ sukhe śrutiḥ āheti peśalaṃ tacca caśabdādeva gamyate  MAnuv rāddhaḥ saṃsiddha ityeva mukta evāvagamyate sādhunā viṣṇunā yukto muktaḥ sādhuyuvā mataḥ  MAnuv yauvanaṃ nityametasya muktasyeti yuvā sa ca phalamadhyayanasyāptaṃ tenādhyāyaka īritaḥ  MAnuv nirhrāsānandasamprāptyā cāśiṣṭa iti gīyate sthitasyānanyathā prāpterdṛḍhiṣṭha iti coditaḥ  MAnuv baliṣṭhaśca svabhāvena mukto bhavati kevalam tasyeyaṃ pṛthivītyādi pūrvabhāvavyapekṣayā  MAnuv sa eka iti saṃsāragatamuktavā sukhaṃ punaḥ śrotriyasyeti vadati muktācchataguṇātmatām  MAnuv saṃsāragācca saṃsāragatasyaiva śatādhikam muktānmuktasya yuktaṃ syācchrutyuktamabhivīkṣitaḥ  MAnuv yuktaṃ ca sādhanādhikyāt sādhyādhikyaṃ surādiṣu nādhikyaṃ yadi sādhye syāt prayatnaḥ sādhane kutaḥ  MAnuv yatnaśca dṛśyate teṣāṃ mahāneva mahātmanām yatra sādhanabāhulyaṃ sādhyabāhulyamatra ca dṛṣṭaṃ niyamato no cenna yatnaṃ kuryarañjasā  MAnuv kṛcchreṇa sādhanādeva na muktavadudīryate daśakalpaṃ tapaścīrṇaṃ rudreṇa lavaṇārṇave tyaktavā sukhāni sarvāṇi kliṣṭena lavaṇāmbhasā  MAnuv śakreṇa varṣakoṭiśca dhūmaḥ pīto tiduḥkhataḥ varṣāyutaṃ ca sūryeṇa tapo vākchirasā kṛtam  MAnuv suduḥkhena sukhaṃ tyaktavā dharmeṇākāśaśāyinā pītā mayīcayo varṣasāhasramatisādaram  MAnuv atikṛcchreṇa kurvanti yatnaṃ brahmavido pi hi ityetadakhilaṃ mokṣaviśeṣābhāvataḥ katham  MAnuv daivī sampad vimokṣāya nibandhāyāsurī matā iti mokṣaviśeṣaśca svayaṃ bhagavatoditaḥ  MAnuv tameva yūyaṃ bhajatātmavṛttibhirmanovacaḥkāyaguṇaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ amāyinaḥ kāmadughāṅghripaṅkajaṃ yathādhikārāvasitārthasiddhaye  MAnuv akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyo manojaveṣvasamā babhūvuḥ ādaghnāsa upakakṣāsa u tve hradā iva snātvā u tve dadṛśre  MAnuv ityādīni ca vākyāni tāratamyaṃ vimuktigam vyaktaṃ vadanti tat kena sāmyaṃ mukteṣu gamyate  MAnuv duḥkhādyabhāvasāmyaṃ ca sāmyavākyārtha īyate bhaktayādiguṇasadbhāve hyatulyatvaṃ ca bhārate uktaṃ sādhanavaiśeṣyamapi sarvatra sattvasthairvyavasāyibhiḥ  MAnuv atītānāgatajñānaprabhavāpyayavedibhiḥ śaucasvādhyāyasantoṣatapassatyadayānvitaiḥ  MAnuv kimu martyairbhayabhrāntidhvaṃsamoharujānvitaiḥ alpāyurvīryadhīsattvavyavasāyaśrutivrataiḥ  MAnuv kastaṃ madāmadaṃ devaṃ madanyo jñātumarhati brahmaiva kiñcijjānāti na tadanyo hi kaścana  MAnuv muktānāmapi siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣvapi mahāmate  MAnuv iyaṃ visṛṣṭiryata ā babhūva yadi vā dadhe yadi vā na yo asyādhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman tso aṅga veda yadi vā na veda  MAnuv yaḥ svātmamāyāvibhavaṃ svayaṃ gato nāhaṃ nabhasvāṃstamathāpare kutaḥ brahmāpi yaṃ vetti naiveha samyaganye kuto devamunīndramartyāḥ  MAnuv namaste mitatattvāya dharmādīnāṃ ca sūtaye nirguṇāya ca satkāṣṭhāṃ nāhaṃ vedāpare kutaḥ  MAnuv nāhaṃ parāyur ṛṣayo na marīcimukhyā jānanti yadviracitaṃ khalu sattvasaṅgāḥ yanmāyayā muṣitacetasa īśadaityamartyādayaḥ kimuta śaśvadabhadravṛttāḥ  MAnuv ahaṃ mahendro nirṛtiḥ pracetāḥ somo gnirīśaḥ pavano rko viriñcaḥ ādityaviśve vasavo tha sādhyā marudgaṇā rudragaṇāḥ sasiddhāḥ  MAnuv anye ca ye viśvasṛjo mareśā bhṛgvādayo spṛṣṭarajastamaskāḥ yasyehitaṃ na viduḥ spṛṣṭṛmāyāḥ sattvapradhānā api kiṃ tato nye  MAnuv savarsyādau smṛto brahmā tasmād devādanantaraḥ jānāti devapravaraṃ bhūyaścāto dhikaṃ nṛpa  MAnuv na tvāmatiśayiṣyanti muktāvapi kathañcana madbhaktiyogājjñānācca sarvānatiśayiṣyasi  MAnuv yathā bhaktiviśeṣo tra dṛśyate puruṣottame tathā muktiviśeṣo pi jñānināṃ liṅgabhedane  MAnuv sāyujyaṃ samanuprāptā api devādayo khilāḥ tāratamyāddhi tiṣṭhanti tāratamyaṃ hi sādhane  MAnuv manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścid yatati siddhaye yatatāmapi siddhānāṃ kaścinmāṃ vetti tattvataḥ  MAnuv ya imaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣvabhidhāsyati bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā māmevaiṣyatyasaṃśayaḥ  MAnuv na ca tasmānmanuṣyeṣu kaścinme priyakṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmādanyaḥ priyataro bhuvi  MAnuv adhyeṣyate ca ya imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃvādamāvayoḥ jñānayajñena tenāhamiṣṭaḥ syāmiti me matiḥ  MAnuv śraddhāvānanasūyuśca śṛṇuyādapi yo naraḥ so pi muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyakarmaṇām  MAnuv dhyānenātmani paśyanti kecidātmānamātmanā anye sāṅkhayena yogena karmayogena cāpare  MAnuv anye tvevamajānantaḥ śrutvānyebhya upāsate te pi cātitarantyeva mṛtyuṃ śrutiparāyaṇāḥ  MAnuv susūkṣmairapyaśeṣaiśca viśeṣaiḥ saha paśyati svātmānaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvarūpo pi sarvadā  MAnuv savartra cānyadapyevaṃ tenādṛṣṭaṃ na hi kvacit sarvatra sarvadaiveśaṃ paśyatyeva ramāpi tu  MAnuv natu sarvairviśeṣaistaṃ paśyantyapyanyato dhikam svātmānamanyaccāśeṣaṃ paśyatyeva hi sarvadā  MAnuv brahmā tu sarvagaṃ paśyed guṇānapyato dhikam natu sarveṣu kāleṣu tathā paśyatyamuktigaḥ  MAnuv muktastu sarvadā paśyet sarvagatvena cāpi tu na ramāvad viśeṣāṇāṃ darśanaṃ śaknuyāt kvacit  MAnuv svātmānamanyacca sadā viśeṣairakhilairapi paśyantyañjastathā vāṇī viśoṣāṃstāvato natu traiguṇyāt parataḥ paśyed vyāptaṃ śataguṇaṃ harim  MAnuv giriśo garuḍaścaiva tamomātragataṃ harim paśyed viśeṣānapi hi vāṇīdṛṣṭān na paśyati  MAnuv umā suparṇī ca mahattattvaṃ yāvat prapaśyati rudradṛṣṭān viśeṣāṃśca naiva paśyet kadācana  MAnuv svarūpamanyarūpaṃ ca muktā devāḥ samastaśaḥ jānantīndraśca kāmaśca brahma yāvadahaṅkṛtiḥ  MAnuv paśyanto manudakṣādyā buddhitattvasthitaṃ harim paśyanti somasūryau tu manasthaṃ parameśvaram  MAnuv anye bhūtasthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ devāḥ paśyanti sarvadā bahusāhasravarṣeṇa mahattattve kvacit kvacit  MAnuv anye caiva yathāyogyamaṇḍāntarvartinaṃ harim śvetadvīpapatiṃ caiva hṛdyevānye tu kecana kadācideva tatrāpi kecit paśyanti keśavam  MAnuv umā yāvadanantāṃśān pūrvadṛṣṭebhya eva tu viśeṣān vāsudevasya paścāduktā vicakṣate  MAnuv śakrakāmādayaścaiva viśeṣān brahmaṇi sthitān umādibhiḥ prabuddhebhyaḥ śatāṃśāneva cakṣate  MAnuv ityādivedasmṛtigavacanebhyo yathārthataḥ tāratamyaṃ vimuktānāṃ sādhanānāṃ ca dṛśyate  MAnuv sādhyasādhanavairūpyamadṛṣṭaṃ kena kalpyate vaiṣamyaṃ nirghṛṇatvaṃ ca tena syātāṃ parasya ca sāpekṣatvāditi ca tau vidyādhīśena vāritau  MAnuv tāratamyāt sādhanānāṃ sādhyatādṛktavamīśataḥ avaiṣamyādihetuḥ syāt sadaiva parameśvare  MAnuv svātantrye vidyamāne pi sādhanādau pareśituḥ apekṣyānādivaicitṛyaṃ na doṣa iti tadvacaḥ nānāditvāditi hyuktamupapadyata ityapi  MAnuv apekṣyopāyavaiṣamyamupeyasya tathā sthitiḥ mayā kayā viruddhā syād rājādāvapi dṛśyate  MAnuv tyāgo dṛṣṭasya cādṛṣṭakalpaneti suduṣkarau māyibhyo nyena kenāpi tat kimanyaiśca vādibhiḥ  MAnuv māyino trānugamyante śrutahānyaśrutagrahau apyatra māyināṃ liṅge tat ke doṣāstato dhikāḥ  MAnuv niśśeṣagatadoṣāṇāṃ bahubhirjanmabhiḥ punaḥ syādāparokṣyaṃ hi harerdveṣerṣyādistataḥ kutaḥ  MAnuv bhaveyuryadi cerṣyādyāḥ sameṣvapi kuto na te tapyamānāḥ samān dṛṣṭvā dveṣerṣyādiyutā api dṛśyante bahavo loke doṣā evātra kāraṇam  MAnuv yadi nirdoṣatā tatra kimādhikyena dūṣyate yadyanyadarśanābhāvādīrṣyādirvinivāryate adarśanādaratyādiḥ kathaṃ tena nivāryate  MAnuv brahmaṇo pyaratirdṛṣṭvā pūrvamekākinaḥ śrutau naiva reme sa caikākī tasamānna ramate kvacit dvitīyamaicchat tenāsāviti śrutaya ūdire  MAnuv yadīcchā tatra naivāstītyeva tat kalpyate mṛṣā śrutyuktanirdoṣataiva kiṃ nāṅgīkriyate svayam  MAnuv tāratamyaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca śrutamevātihāya tu aśrutā samatā kena kalpyate yuktimāninā  MAnuv kiṃ tanmānaṃ samatve te muktānāmupalabhyate vṛthāyamāgrahaḥ kena śrutahānyaśrutagrahe  MAnuv mokṣe pi tāratamyetaścetanatvāt purā yathā ityukta uttaraṃ kiṃ te kalpanāmātravādinaḥ  MAnuv na ca duḥkhādikaṃ kalpyaṃ nirduḥkhatvaśruterbalāt śokaṃ taratyātmavettā tīrṇaḥ sarvānaduḥkhabhāk  MAnuv yenānandyeva bhavati na śocati kadācana kilbiṣaspṛt pituṣaṇiraraṃ hita iheśvaraḥ  MAnuv yaṃ yamantamabhiprepsuḥ sa saṅkalpād bhavediha ityādiśrutayo mānaṃ nirduḥkhatvādisampadi  MAnuv ato duḥkhādyanumayā nāvakāśo tra labhyate tāratamyānumā tena bhavennātiprasaṅginī  MAnuv śrutiyuktibalādevaṃ tāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate muktāvapi tataḥ ke tra virodhaṃ kartumīśate  MAnuv anādiyogyatāṃ caiva kalivāṇīśvarāvadhim ko nivārayituṃ śakto yuktayāgamabaloddhatām  MAnuv brahmaṇo nyatra ādhikyayuktaḥ kālo vivādavān kālo hyayaṃ yathetyādi mānumāmānino bhavet  MAnuv anyaśabdo hariśrīsvasamebhyo nyavivakṣayā prayukto naiva doṣāya rudrādiṣu ca yuktitaḥ  MAnuv uttamatvaṃ tu muktānāmapi na brahmaṇo bhavet vyaktiḥ sukhasya tu bhavennatvādhikyaṃ sukhasya ca  MAnuv balajñānādhikatvaṃ ca tebhyo hi brahmaṇaḥ sadā ādhikyasya tvanityatve na kiñcinmānamīyate  MAnuv śṛṇve vīra ugramugraṃ damāyannanyamanyamatinenīyamānaḥ edhamānadviḷubhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśa indro manuṣyān  MAnuv parā pūrveṣāṃ sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇo aparebhireti anānubhūtīravadhūnvānaḥ pūrvītindraḥ śaradastartarīti  MAnuv divedive sadṛśīranyamardhaṃ kṛṣṇā asedhadapa sadmano jāḥ ahan dāsā vṛṣabho vasnayantodavraje varcinaṃ śambaraṃ ca  MAnuv  taṃ bhūtiriti devā upāsāñcakrire te babhūvustasmāddhāpyetarhi supto bhūbhrūrityeva praśvasityabhūtirityasurāste ha parābabhūvuḥ  MAnuv tad yathā peśaskarī peśaso mātrāmapādāyānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ tanuta evamevāyamātmedaṃśarīraṃ nihatyāvidyāṃ gamayitavānyannavataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ kurute pitṛyaṃ pitṛyaṃvā gāndharvaṃ vā daivaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ vā brāhmaṃ vānyeṣāṃ vā bhūtānām  MAnuv prayānti paramāṃ siddhimaihikāmuṣmikīṃ drutam yā na prāpyāsuraiḥ sarvairakṣayā kleśavarjitā na tāṃ gatiṃ prapadyante vinā bhāgavatān narān  MAnuv avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritam paraṃ bhāvamajānanto mama  MAnuv māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto bhyasūyakāḥ tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu  MAnuv āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani māmaprāpyaiva svādhyāyastattvaveditvaṃ viṣṇupūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ  MAnuv daityānāṃ bāhuṣāḷitvaṃ mātsaryaṃ yuddhasatkriyā nītiśāstrapraveditvaṃ śivapūjāratiḥ smṛtiḥ  MAnuv varṇāśramācāravattvaṃ svādhyāyo bhaktiracyute ityādivākyasandarbhe jñāyate nādiyogyatā  MAnuv yadyanādirviśeṣo na sāmprataṃ kathameva saḥ adṛṣṭādeva cādṛṣṭaṃ svīkṛtaṃ savarvādibhiḥ  MAnuv ākasmiko viśeṣaścedadṛṣṭe kvacidiṣyate sarvatrākasmikatvaṃ bhedena kathañcana pratyabhijñā ca yeṣāṃ na te pi tanmuṣyadṛṣṭayaḥ  MAnuv bhedaṃ naiva prapaśyanti bhedamanyebhya eva ca paśyantyevaṃ haristeṣāṃ sandarśayati nānyathā  MAnuv evaṃ bṛhatsaṃhitāyāṃ vacanaṃ na purāṇagam lokadarśanavādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt  MAnuv aparīkṣitadṛṣṭiśca parīkṣāpūrvadarśanam niṣeddhuṃ śaknuvādyeva vedarodhāya śaknuyāt  MAnuv na ca niścitabhedasya darśane sti viddhavad viṣṇurajāto jātavanmṛṣā abaddho baddhavaccaiva darśayatyamitadyutiḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiścaiva prāha nirdoṣatāṃ hareḥ  MAnuv aparīkṣitadṛṣṭayaiva sadoṣo dṛśyate hariḥ parīkṣādarśane naiva dṛśyo doṣo hareḥ kvacit iti paiṅgiśrutiścāha pramāṇaṃ hi parīkṣitam  MAnuv na parīkṣānavasthā syāt sākṣisiddhe tvasaṃśayāt mānase darśane doṣāḥ syurnavai sākṣidarśane sudṛḍho nirṇayo yatra jñeyaṃ tat sākṣidarśanam  MAnuv icchā jñānaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhabhayābhayakṛpādayaḥ sākṣisiddhā na kaściddhi tatra saṃśayavān kvacit yat kvacid vyabhicārī syād darśanaṃ mānasaṃ hi tat  MAnuv manaścakṣurdarśanāderapi yatraiva sākṣiṇā prāmāṇyaṃ sugṛhītaṃ syāt tat parīkṣitadarśanam  MAnuv na jñānadṛṣṭimātreṇa prāmāṇyaṃ tasya dṛśyate niyamena sukhādyeṣu prāmāṇyaṃ sākṣigocaram  MAnuv svaprāmāṇyaṃ sadā sākṣī paśyatyeva suniścayāt jñānasya grāhakeṇaiva sākṣiṇā mānatāmiteḥ  MAnuv doṣābhāve pramāṇatvaṃ doṣābhāvasya sākṣiṇā niścitatvaṃ kvaciccaiva svataḥ prāmāṇyamiṣyate  MAnuv ato na sarvamānānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ niścitaṃ bhavet sākṣiṇā niścitaṃ yatra tat prāmāṇyasvalakṣaṇam  MAnuv na hi kaścit sukhādyeṣu saṃśayaṃ kurute janaḥ nacaivākhilamānāni niścinotyakhilo janaḥ  MAnuv tasmādanubhavārūḍhaṃ kimarthamupalapyate doṣābhāvādikaṃ caiva sākṣī samyak prapaśyati  MAnuv tat parīkṣitamānena na doṣo viṣṇavi kvacit aparīkṣitadṛṣṭistu kasminnarthe na vidyate  MAnuv tat pratyakṣaviruddhārthe nāgamasyāpi mānatā
